League of Nations Committee of Nineteen

Resolution Draft Passed

Empty Content Just to Deal with the Situation

Great Powers’ Pro-Japanese Attitude Unchanged

U.S. and Russia’s Participation Uncertain

Our Country Only Has Two Paths to Follow

Firmly Unyielding or Offered as a Sacrifice

Mexico, Angered by Great Powers’ Oppression of Small Countries, Notifies Withdrawal from League of Nations

(Geneva) The Committee of Nineteen passed the draft resolution of the Drafting Committee today. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) The five-member Drafting Committee continued to meet for three days. Due to differences of opinion between large and small countries, heated debates arose repeatedly. Only before the meeting of the Committee of Nineteen this afternoon did the Drafting Committee agree on a draft resolution, which reportedly includes the following points: 1. The basis of the principle of mediation; 2. The procedure for inviting the U.S. and Russia; 3. The issue of accepting the Lytton Report. This draft will be passed by the Committee of Nineteen and submitted to the League of Nations General Assembly for discussion after being sent to both China and Japan. However, because Russia seems to be refusing to participate and the U.S.'s participation is uncertain, the future is extremely difficult. Although the League of Nations wants to use its power to implement reconciliation, the great powers’ pro-Japanese attitude has not changed. China only has two paths to take: one is to firmly unyielding, and the other is to be offered as a sacrifice. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) The Drafting Committee established by the League of Nations' Committee of Nineteen held meetings twice today, in the morning and afternoon, to discuss the resolution issue. At the meeting, British Foreign Secretary Simon continued to pressure the representatives of the Czech Republic and Spain to maintain justice and strongly advocated yielding to Japan. Therefore, the resolution was shortened to two pages, with content that merely dealt with the situation and thanked the Lytton mission for their efforts. It advocated that the Committee of Nineteen be changed into a Mediation Committee. Because Japan opposed the proposal to invite the U.S. and Russia, Simon, having received a request from Japan, also advocated deleting this item. As for whether the invitation to the U.S. and Russia can be successful, it will only be decided at the meeting at 3:30 PM on the 15th. It is expected that the meeting will be concluded by 5 PM on the 15th. The British Foreign Secretary Simon, who is acting as an accomplice to Japan, returned to England at 10:45 PM today. It is generally speculated that Simon has succeeded in pressuring the small countries. (China United Press dispatch, 14th)

(Geneva) The representatives of England, France, the Czech Republic, Spain, and Switzerland, the five-member Drafting Committee, finalized the proposal and report draft today, which will be considered by the Committee of Nineteen at its meeting at 5 PM this afternoon and then sent to the representatives of China and Japan. When the Drafting Committee was discussing, the Japanese representative Sato sat in an adjacent room, and the Drafting Committee members frequently went back and forth. The Drafting Committee is currently keeping the contents of the draft strictly secret, but it is heard that the wording is very mild. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) The Drafting Committee elected by the Committee of Nineteen seemed to have encountered difficulties yesterday, and the draft resolution it prepared was therefore delayed until noon today to be finalized. Even if the Committee of Nineteen can make a decision today, the representatives of China and Japan must first consult their respective governments before convening an extraordinary assembly. Therefore, it is generally believed that the extraordinary assembly may not be able to hold a meeting at the beginning of next week. As for the content of the draft resolution, it is merely a reiteration of the resolution of the General Assembly on March 11th of this year. The issue of inviting the U.S. and Russia to participate will be decided by the extraordinary assembly. Although British Foreign Secretary Simon is an important figure in the drafting of the resolution, he is not presiding over it. Simon has already left Geneva last night, and the British representative Kagan is acting on his behalf. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Tokyo) According to a Geneva dispatch, the resolution drafted by the Drafting Committee on the 13th is only two pages long, and the content seems simple and indifferent. The result of British Foreign Secretary Simon's efforts to suppress the representatives of small countries and exclude resolutions unfavorable to Japan is clearly visible. The main points are as follows: 1. Reaffirmation of the General Assembly's resolution on March 11th; 2. Supporting the Lytton Report's agreement on the Sino-Japanese issue and providing the best information; 3. Raising the issue of a Mediation Committee, but not mentioning the invitation to the U.S. and Russia. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 15th)

U.S. and Russia Participation Issue

League of Nations Telegraphs Washington to Solicit Opinions

Russia Expresses Unwillingness to Participate in Mediation

(Geneva) From the perspective of observation, Russia seems unwilling to participate in the Committee of Nineteen. As for the U.S., it must first know the basic conditions for mediating the Sino-Japanese issue before agreeing to participate. Last night, the League of Nations telegraphed Washington to solicit opinions. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Mexico Notifies Withdrawal from League of Nations

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat received a letter from the Mexican government this morning, stating that due to financial difficulties, the country fears that it will be unable to pay membership fees in the near future, so it has no choice but to withdraw from the League of Nations after giving two years' notice, as required by the covenant. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) At 3 PM this afternoon, the Mexican representative to Geneva visited Drummond, stating that Mexico will withdraw from the League of Nations. Although Mexico uses the inability to afford League of Nations fees as the reason, the truth is not that simple. It is said that Mexico has seen through the League of Nations as merely a tool for England and France to oppress small countries and is completely manipulated by the European Union. Joining is no longer beneficial and is detrimental in spirit, so it cannot but withdraw frankly. If the League of Nations cannot uphold justice in the Sino-Japanese dispute in the future, it is feared that Mexico will not be the only country to withdraw from the League of Nations. (China United Press dispatch, 14th)

British Side Explains Misunderstanding to Us

Simon's Remarks Did Not Show Partiality?

(Nanjing) Since the British representative Simon made pro-Japanese remarks at the League of Nations General Assembly, which were unanimously criticized by our country's public opinion, the British side has somewhat awakened. It is reliably learned that the British government has indirectly and directly expressed to our government authorities that Simon's remarks at the League of Nations General Assembly were intended to promote reconciliation and did not show partiality to any party. England is a loyal member of the League of Nations and will not lag behind in maintaining the dignity of the covenant. It hopes that China will not misunderstand this. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

True Face of British Imperialism

Anglo-Persian Oil Case

Rushed to Invoke Article 15 of the Covenant

(Geneva) The Chinese delegation to the League of Nations feels that England is strict with itself and lenient with others, because England is eager to invoke Article 15 of the covenant in the dispute over the Anglo-Persian oil concession, while China has more than enough reason to invoke this article, but England has suggested to China that it endure Japanese aggression. The general opinion is that England and Persia only have a dispute over economic issues, and now they are eagerly proposing Article 15 of the covenant as a response. This move, in spirit, can consolidate the position of the Chinese delegation at the extraordinary assembly. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Simon Hastens Back to London

Japanese Representatives Lobby Late at Night

(London) British Foreign Secretary Simon returned from Geneva and arrived in London by plane at 11:20 this morning. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) Representative Matsuoka and Ambassador Matsudaira to England visited British Foreign Secretary Simon, who was about to return home, at his hotel at 9:40 PM on the 14th, explaining that Japan will absolutely not change its League of Nations countermeasures for any changes in the meeting, and exchanged opinions on the Drafting Committee of the resolution before departing at 10:50 PM. After the meeting, Matsuoka told Japanese reporters that he made a special trip to pay his respects because Sir Simon was about to return home, and at the same time exchanged opinions on two or three points. (Dentsu dispatch, 15th)

(Tokyo) Geneva dispatch: Japanese representative Matsudaira met with British Foreign Secretary Simon twice on the 14th, in the morning and afternoon, to explain Japan's position. Matsudaira had always been in contact with Simon, so after Simon returned home, Matsudaira also returned to England from Geneva to take up his post. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Shandong Provincial Party Department Consoles Three Representatives

(Jinan) The Shandong Provincial Party Department telegraphed representatives Yan, Gu, and Guo in Geneva on the 13th, stating that at this League of Nations meeting, the officials, entrusted by the people and shouldering the mission of the nation, attended the meeting, negotiated, exposed the conspiracy of the violent Japan, and strongly refuted Matsuoka's sophistry. They were righteous and eloquent, arousing sympathy from friendly nations and jointly condemning the Japanese atrocities. Although the final victory is still unknown, the officials' hard work is truly commendable. Separated by the ocean, we cannot help but express our admiration and telegraph our condolences, hoping that they will continue their efforts. (Special dispatch, 15th)

Dr. Nitobe Inazo Strives to Promote Propaganda to the U.S.

(Washington) U.S. Senator Borah inquired in the Senate today about the opinions on quickly proceeding with the recognition of Russia. As for whether England and France's attitude towards us will change, conventionally speaking, the resumption of relations between Country A and Country B in the international community is not enough to attract the attention of other countries or change attitudes. In my opinion, England and France both occupy important positions in our country's commerce, and I think they will not voluntarily give up their inherent goodwill and help the wicked. But based on past and recent events, in terms of morality and justice, England and France have not been righteous speakers, which is regrettable. As for the U.S. and Russia's expression of unwillingness to participate in the Committee of Nineteen, it is because they see that the League of Nations has repeatedly evaded responsibility in handling the Sino-Japanese issue, so it cannot attract non-member countries to join hands willingly. Those who are not careful in their comments may say that the League of Nations intends to shift responsibility to the U.S. and Russia, which is excessive, but it is not unworthy of consideration. However, for its own sake, the League of Nations should not show weakness because of the U.S. and Russia's non-participation. Wang did not say that our country has lost several provinces, and the aggressor has not shown the slightest sign of remorse. If we still rely on the League of Nations without preparing for practical strength and national unity, I am afraid that the Northeast territory will never be ours. (Special dispatch, 15th)

Russian Newspaper Mocks Japan

Resumption of Relations Only to Consolidate Peace

Japanese Statements are Contradictory

(Moscow) The Soviet government newspaper "Izvestia" commented in an editorial today on the Japanese Foreign Ministry spokesperson's remarks on the Sino-Russian resumption of relations, saying that the Japanese Foreign Ministry spokesperson described the terror and threat of the Sino-Russian resumption of relations to Japan as being expressed to the fullest. These remarks lack the cultivation and composure of Japanese diplomats. There is nothing special about the resumption of normal relations between China and Russia. This move is only to consolidate peace and create a stable situation. Furthermore, the Japanese spokesperson's remarks are contradictory. China and the Soviet Union maintaining normal relations is a "big mistake," while Japan and the Soviet Union maintaining normal relations is completely legitimate, the distinction between which is quite puzzling. The Soviet Union has always adhered to a peaceful policy and is willing to maintain normal relations with all countries. The Sino-Russian resumption of relations is a clear manifestation of the peaceful policy and has no other peculiarities. It is clear that the "terror" and "threat" theories of some Japanese newspapers have seen their impact on the psychology of Japanese government officials. Finally, the newspaper expressed surprise at the Japanese statement that the Sino-Russian resumption of relations reduces the possibility of concluding a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty, saying that "Does this statement indicate that Japan will create new reasons to insist on rejecting the non-aggression treaty proposed by the Soviet Union? If so, then this statement is even more contradictory. The Soviet Union is still willing to conclude a non-aggression treaty with Japan and Manchuria. If Japan is indeed harboring the views on the Sino-Russian resumption of relations made by its Foreign Ministry spokesperson, then it can directly conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union and eliminate all unfounded suspicions." (TASS dispatch, 14th)

Regulations on Repaying Accumulated Debts by the Puppet Organization

(Changchun) The "Manchukuo" government, due to the Manchurian Incident and the demise of the Northeastern regime, faced demands for payment of unpaid debts and other similar arrears. To resolve this, a Committee for Post-Incident Debt Settlement was established. A solution has been reached, announced by Chairman Sakatani as follows: 1. For goods delivered after 1930 for which payment has not yet been made, totaling over 7,110,000 yuan, 35% will be repaid in the "first year of Datong," approximately 2,500,000 yuan, and 25% in the "second year of Datong," approximately 1,500,000 yuan, both in cash. The remaining amount will be paid with two-year bonds of the same face value, bearing 2% interest. 2. For debts incurred before 1929 and for undelivered goods, totaling approximately 1,200,000 yuan, a reasonable decision will be made after investigation. It is provisionally planned to issue bonds with the same terms as above, equivalent to the amount of the debt or the damages. All creditors, both domestic and foreign, will be treated equally. (15th Teletype from Dentsu)

(Yantai) At 5:40 PM tonight, a large amount of ammunition suddenly exploded in the western suburbs of Yantai, followed by a large fire. Smaller explosions occurred repeatedly, ceasing only at night. The force of the first explosion was extremely violent, shattering glass windows three miles away, and artillery shell fragments flew into the air, falling into the port. Residents were greatly shocked, but soon learned the truth and calmed down. (15th Reuters Teletype)

(Yantai) Further information: Tonight's explosion originated under the stone embankment west of Yantai, where a large number of bullets were piled up, including 300 mortar shells. Summary of the Restructuring of Party Affairs by Headquarters

Hubei Provincial Party Department Requests Instructions

Recognizing the Difficulties in Implementing the Summary

(Hankou) The Provincial Party Department presented a report to the Third Plenary Session and the Central Committee on the 15th, requesting instructions on the summary of the restructuring of party affairs issued by the Headquarters. It stated, "Since the Headquarters announced the summary, party members have been confused, the people are concerned, and reactionary elements are spreading rumors that our party is incapable of leadership and is about to be abolished, resulting in a sharp decline in public trust in the party. The committee dares not comply with the letter from the Headquarters, and yet cannot afford to not comply. After consideration, it was decided to request instructions. The power to amend the general regulations belongs to the National Congress. The summary seems to differ in many ways from the general regulations. In terms of powers, the county party department can audit the policy direction of the same-level government, but the summary contains no such provision. In terms of discipline, if a party member has not violated party discipline, then a legally formed party department cannot dissolve it. In terms of the system, all working comrades in party departments at all levels are appointed by higher levels. If recommendations are submitted to the Headquarters for approval, it does not seem to be the appropriate procedure. In terms of mission, if party members delve into the masses, then according to the summary, the party will be isolated from the masses. The committee believes all of this is difficult to implement. We believe that Chiang embraces party rule, surpassing ordinary people, and that his demands are strict. We are afraid he is correcting wrongs to an extreme. These are temporary changes within the party, but outside the party, they aim to fundamentally destroy. We ask for a detailed review." The Hankou Municipal Party Department will also submit a similar petition requesting instructions. (15th Dispatch)

It exploded at the time, injuring the shop's worker Shi Yongfu, who was sent to the hospital for treatment. The police arrived at the scene after the incident to investigate. The bomber has fled without a trace. (15th Dispatch)

(Zhenjiang) On the 15th, the Construction Department dispatched Liu Chunzhong, Yu Liming, Cao Guang, Zhang Youbin, and Huang Qibin to take over the Industry Department. If there is no increase in funding afterwards, the department's monthly expenses can be reduced by 19,000 yuan, and the affiliated agencies by 20,000 yuan. (15th Dispatch)

He visited President Dai's prayer hall and talked for half an hour, then went to the Central Party Headquarters to attend the opening ceremony of the plenary session. (15th Dispatch)

They are scheduled to take the original train to Zhengzhou on the 16th and transfer to Luoyang. (15th Central News Agency Teletype)

War Debt Disputes Emerge One After Another

Britain and Italy Pay as Planned, France and Belgium Stop Payment

Eastern European Countries Also Have Problems

War Debt Reorganization Negotiations to Begin Next Spring

The National News Agency telegraphed from Washington on the 14th, stating that the State Department announced today that the US government will adopt a wait-and-see policy regarding France and Belgium's failure to pay war debts on time. Both countries have notified the State Department that they will not be able to repay as scheduled. Britain's decision to pay the war debt as scheduled tomorrow has created a good impression in the United States. Negotiations to study Britain's entire war debt structure are expected to begin in early spring next year.

▲Reuters telegraphed from London on the 14th that today's newspapers carried news that British cabinet members will travel to Washington at the beginning of the new year to discuss the revision of debts between Britain and the United States. Political circles hope that the new and old presidents of the United States, Roosevelt and Hoover, can cooperate with each other in this conversation.

▲The National News Agency telegraphed from Washington on the 14th that after the British and Italian war debts due tomorrow have been paid, it is expected that the war debt issue will not be mentioned again in this session of Congress. Any motion to adjust war debt repayment will be handled by the next session of Congress. According to the current situation, the next session of Congress will convene around March or April, at which time nearly one-third of the House of Representatives members will be replaced with new figures, and most of them will be Democrats, who are expected to follow the lead of the new President Roosevelt.

▲Reuters telegraphed from Washington on the 14th that Republican Senator Keener today introduced a bill in the House of Representatives to prohibit the inflow of bonds of foreign governments that do not repay their debts into the United States and to prohibit the advertisement and transportation of such bonds.

US Attitude Towards France

Reuters telegraphed from Washington on the 14th that the US government's attitude towards European countries regarding debt repayment or overdue issues remains unchanged, despite France's strong advocacy for convening a meeting. However, there is an undercurrent of unease in political circles. News from France indicates that unless the United States agrees to reconsider, the French Chamber of Deputies will resolutely oppose payment. Democratic Senator McClellan expressed indignation today at France's behavior, saying that he believes this is the most indecent thing done by any country in the world, indicating that European countries treat treaty obligations as waste paper, and not just Germany. Chairman McKinley of the House Foreign Affairs Committee said that France's reasons for not paying war debts are not as good as any other country, because what it should pay is only 75% of what it received after the war. As for France's ability to pay the debt, it is not a problem. The White House and the State Department are still silent on this issue.

British and Italian Payment Methods

Havas telegraphed from New York on the 14th that general opinion on Wall Street here seems to believe that France's attitude has little impact on finance. The New York Federal Reserve Bank has confirmed the method adopted by Britain to repay the US debt of US$95,550,000, which is that the New York Reserve Bank will allocate cash for the British government's disposal, and then the Bank of England will record the amount in the US account for future remittance.

▲Reuters telegraphed from Rome on the 14th that it was announced in Rome today that Italy is prepared to repay the US debt of 1,245,000 yuan due tomorrow, and has now officially made good preparations for repayment.

France Has Notified of Non-Payment

Havas telegraphed from Washington on the 14th that the French Ambassador to the United States, Claudel, delivered a note to Secretary of State Stimson at 6:00 PM today, stating that the French government now has no authority to consult with the United States on war debt issues.

Problems Also Arise in Eastern Europe

Havas telegraphed from the Romanian capital on the 14th that the Foreign Minister recently ordered the Romanian Minister to the United Kingdom to contact British Prime Minister MacDonald regarding the Eastern European reparations issue. The grace period for this payment will expire tomorrow. The Lausanne Conference previously decided to have a special meeting to resolve this matter, but this meeting was never convened. The purpose of this contact is to seek an extension of the grace period.

▲Havas telegraphed from Warsaw on the 14th that the United States had stipulated that Poland's debt of 27 million Polish currency should be repaid in a certain form. Poland has recently decided not to repay in the scheduled form, but to show its sincerity, it will find a compromise repayment plan, or pay a portion first, or request repayment with promissory notes.

▲Havas telegraphed from Warsaw on the 14th that the Estonian government had previously requested the United States to allow it to postpone the payment of debt due on the 15th of this month. The United States did not reply. According to a report by the Polish Batalion News Agency, the Estonian government has decided not to pay.

The French Government Formation Stalled

The President Spends the Day Soliciting Opinions from Various Parties

Paris, 15th (National News Agency) - All eyes are currently focused on the meeting between the French President and Herriot this afternoon. At that time, the President will ask Herriot to form a new cabinet based on the majority opinion of the party leaders. However, it is generally speculated that Herriot may refuse to form a cabinet. Others suggest that the Radical Socialist Party should ask other leaders to form a new cabinet, still based on the previous cabinet's foundation in the National Assembly.

▲ Paris, 15th (National News Agency) - Although the Herriot cabinet has fallen, Herriot's prestige has greatly increased due to his heroic performance in the National Assembly yesterday. Almost the entire country believes that he is the only person capable of leading the country and safely navigating the difficult situation after the National Assembly rejected the debt repayment. If he strongly refuses to reorganize a new cabinet at this time, the cabinet crisis may be prolonged for several days or even a week or more.

▲ Paris, 14th (Reuters) - The French President has been very busy contacting important figures from various political parties today, but a successor has not yet been decided. After meeting with the President this afternoon, the Chairman of the Finance Committee, Mars, told people, "The difficult political situation has just begun, and Herriot has not lost any of his authority." This statement almost implies inviting Herriot to cooperate in forming a new cabinet. There is now much talk of organizing a new government with the same colors as the Herriot cabinet, with the intention of having Paul-Boncour, Chautemps, Caillaux, or Steeg as Prime Minister. It is found that the above-mentioned people all belong to the Radical Party, similar to Herriot. It is expected that the President will first ask Herriot to reorganize the cabinet, but Herriot may temporarily decline until others have tried and then decide what to do.

George Bernard Shaw Departs for China

He Proposes "Gifting Ireland to the United States to Offset War Debts"

London, 15th (Havas News Agency) - The literary giant George Bernard Shaw and his wife left London this morning for a trip around the world. Shaw is a witty Irish writer whose footprints are all over the globe. He apparently does not intend to visit his hometown. When asked why he was not going to Ireland, Shaw replied, "I can make a suggestion to gift Ireland to the United States to offset war debts."

Why Did Puyi's Brother-in-Law Come to London?

No Outsiders Allowed Near His Residence

London, 15th (Reuters) - Puyi's brother-in-law, Mr. Zheng, and his wife have arrived here. According to Zheng's words to guests, they are here as students, and their main purpose is to learn English and investigate the situation of British society. As for how long they will stay in England, it cannot be predetermined and depends on the situation in China. Mr. and Mrs. Zheng are currently being hosted by Sir Johnston, Puyi's former English teacher.

▲ London, 15th (Reuters) - Mr. and Mrs. Zheng are currently residing at Johnston's residence. Johnston is protecting them thoroughly, not allowing outsiders to approach. Even friends who want to enter his house are turned away.

Belgium Forms New Government

Brussels, 14th (National News Agency) - Belgian Prime Minister de Broqueville resigned yesterday due to changes in the composition of the National Assembly, but today he was re-appointed by the King to form a new cabinet. De Broqueville has accepted the mandate. It is said that de Broqueville is now planning to form a national coalition cabinet. The previous cabinet only included figures from the Catholic Party and the Liberal Party. This time, the Socialist Party will be added. It is expected that the list of candidates for the new cabinet will be submitted to the King for approval on Friday.

U.S. Congress Discusses Philippine Independence Bill

It Is Too Early to Say It Will Be Passed

Washington, 14th (National News Agency) - Today, the U.S. Senate passed the Broussard Amendment to the Hare–Hawes–Cutting Act for Philippine independence. The content stipulates an eight-year transition period before independence is implemented. During this period, all Philippine goods will be subject to import duties, with the tax rate increasing annually. Initially, a 5% ad valorem tax will be levied, and in the final year, the highest tax rate can be increased to 85%. In the previous Congress, this amendment was considered too radical, and some senators believed that the eight-year preparation period was too short, so it failed to pass. Now, with the pro-independence forces greatly increased, it was quickly passed. After this amendment was passed, Senator Pittman immediately moved to adopt the Hare bill passed by the House of Representatives. Because the House bill is not much different from the amended Senate bill, it can save negotiation procedures by passing the House bill. Currently, this motion is still being voted on. However, regardless of whether the Senate adopts its own bill or the House's Hare bill, the independence of the Philippines can definitely be passed by both houses and transferred to the President within a few days. Because of the current situation in the Senate, it is expected that there will be an overwhelming majority in favor of independence.

▲ Washington, 14th (National News Agency) - Today, Washington was quite surprised to receive widespread news from abroad that the U.S. Congress has agreed to Philippine independence within eight years. Because Pittman's motion in the Senate has not yet been voted on. Although the Senate's adoption of the Broussard Amendment shows support for Philippine independence within a shorter period of time, the entire bill has not yet been decided. It cannot be hastily said that Congress has agreed to the Philippine independence bill within eight years.

Switzerland Elects New President

Bern, 15th (National News Agency) - The Swiss Federal Council and the two chambers of parliament held a joint meeting today and elected Federal Councillor Edmund Schulthess as the Swiss Federal President for 1933 and Philipp Etter as Vice President.

Japanese Police Forbid Taiwanese People from Mining Gold Dust

Hualien, 15th (Japan News Agency) - The waves on the east coast of Taiwan have been very strong recently. Many gold dusts were found on the coast of Hualien Port. Tribal residents secretly went to explore and extract them at night. After the police authorities found out, they confiscated the gold mining equipment and sent people to monitor the coast.

The Northeast Problem and the League of Nations (2)

The War of Words Between the Chinese and Japanese Representatives in the Investigative Committee

In the afternoon, the Chinese representative, Dr. Wellington Koo, stated that he reserved the right to refute the Japanese representative's attacks on China. Regarding the Japanese representative's use of the Kellogg-Briand Pact to embellish his aggression as self-defense, he asked those present who had signed the pact to judge for themselves. Then, he detailed China's position on the Northeast problem, from the historical facts of Japan's invasion of China since ancient times to the completion of the Investigative Committee's report, for two hours. He asked the League of Nations to seek a fundamental solution based on the Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Lytton Report. The full text is as follows:

Before stating the views of the Chinese government, I would like to address what the Japanese representative said this morning. If we were to accept everything the Japanese representative said, then Japan would be a docile sheep being bitten by a ferocious China, trying its best to escape in order to survive. Fortunately, the Administrative Yuan has the Investigative Committee's report as evidence, because the content of the report is completely impartial and fair. The Japanese representative raised several points in his speech this morning, which are the same points that I am about to mention. However, there are other points, as well as the points in the "Opinion Book" that was just published last night, which I will criticize next time. The most shocking thing in the Japanese representative's speech was the criticism of the current situation of the Chinese government. On this point, I will explain the reasons why the Japanese government has been constantly attacking China. Even if we assume, for the sake of discussion, that what the Japanese government said is not completely inaccurate, we should still ask whether the Japanese government's military aggression and the military occupation of the richest three eastern provinces of China, which have a national border area equal to the territory of France and Germany, can be considered justified. The Japanese representative also claimed that the actions of the Japanese army in the three eastern provinces were only acts of self-defense, and cited the reservations specially put forward by the major signatories of the Kellogg-Briand Pact to justify them. However, the Japanese representative also claimed that the Japanese military had long planned in detail. With one call to action, the entire army rose up. Their actions were almost automatic. The Japanese representative expressed his satisfaction with the rapid and precise implementation of the plan. However, the Japanese representative forgot to point out that the Chinese side had absolutely no plans for aggression or self-defense. All of this has been confirmed by the Lytton Report. On the night of September 18th to the 19th, when the Japanese army used machine guns and artillery to implement its planned plan, the Chinese army automatically withdrew and did not make any resistance. Just from this point, can we still regard the actions of the Japanese army as acts of self-defense? If the actions of the Japanese army, as the Japanese representative said, can be regarded as acts of self-defense within the scope of the reservations of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, then why do we need to maintain this peace pact? However, I firmly believe that some of you in the Administrative Yuan who personally participated in the establishment of the pact will have a better explanation. I can only ask you to explain it yourself. I have made the above-mentioned remarks on the Japanese representative's speech, and now I would like to present the Chinese government's views on the Investigative Committee's report to the Administrative Yuan. The crystallization of the work of the Investigative Committee, that is, its report to the Administrative Yuan, should receive the greatest praise. The Chinese people express sincere respect to Lord Lytton and his colleagues, as well as the secretaries, experts, and other staff of the Investigative Committee for completing their important mission, and it is appropriate. I would like to take this opportunity to formally express the Chinese government's admiration. During the nine months of hard work, the Investigative Committee did not change its enthusiasm for the cause due to changes in the environment and climate. As the Chinese representative, I followed the gentlemen and was especially honored to witness their sincerity, perseverance, and sense of responsibility. The Investigative Committee was quite concerned about the unnecessary obstacles to the Chinese representative's accompanying them to the three eastern provinces. After the Chinese representative and his entourage arrived in the three eastern provinces, various unexpected restrictions emerged one after another. All actions were restricted, so that the Chinese representative could not provide assistance within the scope of his duties during the local investigation by the Investigative Committee, as stipulated in the resolution of the Administrative Yuan on December 10 last year. Several times, the Chinese representative had to ask the Investigative Committee to pay attention to the various difficulties and inconveniences he and his entourage were experiencing. These difficulties and inconveniences were sufficient to unnecessarily restrict his freedom of action and hinder the execution of his mission. I remember that the Chinese representative made a public letter to the Investigative Committee on April 27 this year in Shenyang, which said,

'Whenever any member of the Chinese representative went out, one or more Japanese policemen would follow behind. Inside the Yamato Hotel, there were also many Japanese policemen circulating and monitoring. When the Chinese representative moved from one room to another or entered the dining room for meals, someone followed behind. The room numbers of the rooms that the Chinese representative entered and exited were also registered. Part of the Chinese delegation resided in the Toyo Hotel, and the situation was even more difficult. There were about ten Japanese policemen monitoring at the bottom level. When members of the Chinese delegation went out, they had to notify the detectives in the hotel so that they could send someone to "protect" them. Even in private rooms in the hotel, there could never be a moment of peace. Japanese policemen could break into the room at any time to ask questions to members of the delegation. The Chinese delegation was completely isolated from foreign contacts. Chinese people were absolutely not allowed to go to the Yamato Hotel or the Toyo Hotel to visit the delegation, and all Chinese people who did so were arrested.'

Fierce Fighting Before Su Bingwen's Retreat

The Japanese Army's Attempt to Lure Su Failed, So They Launched a Large-Scale Attack

Zhalantun Was Attacked by Surprise, So the Soviet Army Began to Retreat

Harbin Correspondence: In the battle on the Haman Line, the Japanese army entered Lantun at noon on December 1. A column of armored vehicles advanced north from Zhalantun on the afternoon of the 1st, intending to attack the Xing'an Mountains and Boketu. Our National Salvation Army, led by Su Bingwen and Zhang Dianjiu, ordered the troops in front to retreat and defend the Xing'an Mountains, while also rushing to transfer troops from the rear to concentrate at Mandu River and Hailar. Both sides are actively preparing, hoping that the Japanese army will not attack the Xing'an Mountains within a week. Because after the fierce battle at Fularji, Yaokule, and Houkuler on November 10, the National Salvation Army heavily concentrated its forces, with Zhang Yuding's troops concentrated to defend Gefen Mountain, confronting the Japanese army in Yaokule and Houkuler. Wu Delin's army defended Zhujia Kan, and Mongolian cavalry guarded Nianzishan and Genghis Khan. The general headquarters was set up in Lantun, and Zhang Dianjiu borrowed Xie Ke to plan military affairs there. However, the National Salvation Army was weak, with less than 5,000 troops in total. Once dispersed, it became more inconvenient to communicate and respond. Su Bingwen's intention was that the Japanese side had sent Komatsubara, the chief of the Harbin Special Affairs Agency, as a negotiator, and invited him to meet at Manchuria, a border town on the Soviet-Russian border, to ask for the release of Japanese expatriates who were banned in Manchuria. He intended to use this point to play along, waiting for the end of the League of Nations conference before planning further development. He knew that his troops were not many and lacked weapons. Once a fire was started, the Japanese army would heavily concentrate its forces and increase them continuously, so it would be difficult for the National Salvation Army to deal with it for a long time. Therefore, although he was not very willing to attend the meeting that Komatsubara hoped for, he successively released 48 Japanese expatriate women and children from Manchuria to ease the military situation. Komatsubara arrived at the Russian border on November 13 and has been there for two weeks. During this time, a plane had flown into Russian territory once and was once expelled by the Soviet-Russian authorities, saying that Su Bingwen had no intention of negotiating, so the Japanese side's committee had no need to stay. The Japanese felt quite embarrassed by this, but they had to shamelessly stay in Russia for a few more days. On the one hand, their Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, Mr. Isoya, reported to the country and held a special military conference, deciding to attack and aim at the Xing'an Mountains. Then, heavy troops would be sent to force Su Bingwen to submit and release the Japanese expatriates. This was the first step. After Su released the Japanese expatriates, they would send troops to attack Su, determined to eliminate Su's power. In order to avoid contact with Russia, the army targeted Cuogang between Manchuria. Another branch of Zhang HaiPeng's Mongolian army was transferred to bypass the Xing'an Mountains from the Suolun Mountain grassland to cut off the connection between Hailar and Nianzishan and Zhalantun. The troop deployment was as follows: The Hiraga Brigade was responsible for the front, advancing along the railway from Fularji. The Hattori Brigade of the 6th Korean Division, newly transferred from the east, was the main force, taking Gannannan (i.e., Ganjingzi) from Qiqihar, bypassing our army's three lines of defense on Gefen Mountain, Nianzishan, and Zhujia Kan, and attacking the rear of Zhalantun. Another cavalry unit was the reserve force, taking our Genghis Khan position. The Motegi Regiment took the Nianzishan position, and the Miyamoto Branch took the Gefen Mountain position. The total strength of the troops was more than 16,000, with advanced weapons such as armored vehicles and airplanes attached. On November 29, our army detected the increase of the Japanese army and once attacked Fularji with armored vehicles and destroyed the railway south of Zhujia Kan to block the Japanese army's advance. At the same time, all armies were also actively preparing for an all-out attack, intending to launch a counterattack. However, because the troops were too small, once they were transferred, the rear was in danger, so the counterattack was not carried out. After the Japanese army's plan reached Qiqihar, it began to operate under the command of the 14th Division Commander, Matsuki Naoaki. The Hattori Brigade, which departed from Qiqihar, requisitioned hundreds of large and small cars from Heiyuan, and transported them overnight on the 29th. By the morning of the 30th, it had advanced to the northeastern highlands of Zhalantun. Although Zhalantun was our army's general headquarters, there were not many troops there. After discovering the enemy army appearing in the rear, they had to issue a retreat order, retreating to the city of Zhalantun (i.e., Yalu County). A fierce battle broke out with the Japanese army outside the city. The Japanese army responded with air and land forces, attacking from above and below. Our army fought fiercely for two hours. At about 10 o'clock on this day, they retreated to the grassland. Our army in Nianzishan, Genghis Khan, and Gefen Mountain heard that the enemy army had appeared in the rear, so they had to abandon the forward positions and withdraw outside the railway. The Japanese army took the opportunity to occupy Nianzishan and Genghis Khan, and used several airplanes near Boketu to chase and bomb trains and destroy railways, cutting off our army's retreat route. Now, our armies are retreating along the Mongolian grassland, and their strength has not been greatly damaged. Su Bingwen heard the news and led thousands of troops to the Xing'an Mountains to defend that area to prevent the enemy army from advancing again. However, since the Japanese army has bypassed to the rear, it is afraid that it will be difficult to defend for a long time. Su had a letter to the elders of the Northeast a few days ago, which was found in Harbin, advising the people to help with money if they have money, and to destroy the enemy's rear if they have strength. The letter was sent by the post office and was seized by the Japanese side. It said that Manchuria could no longer send mail. The discovery of this printed matter was probably due to local people advertising for Su. Because a certain brigade commander (said to be Li Wenbing) who is now serving the puppet state is being monitored, the traitors of the puppet state are now in danger. (December 3)

The Soviet Construction Department Takes Over the Industry Department

After the Industry Department of Jiangsu Province was ordered to close down and was taken over by the Construction Department, it was heard that the Construction Department, in order to save money, intends to merge the original Section 5 Affairs Section into Section 4 after taking over the Industry Department. All the affairs of the Industry Department will be merged into the respective sections of the Construction Department in order. In addition, no new sections will be set up. As for the position of section chief, in the future, the original Section 5 Chief Yu Liming may be appointed as the chief of Section 4, and the original Section 4 Chief Liu Chunzhong will be transferred to Section 5. The Construction Department has now assigned ten people, including technician Tang Youguang, to take over successively from today. Very few of the original employees of the Industry Department will be hired. As for technicians and engineers, they need to be recruited. Other important employees will be carefully re-employed based on their talents, about a dozen people, and the rest will be appointed from within the department or transferred from other sections. Suzhou

Approval Document for the Robbery of the Yutai Steamboat

The Yutai steamboat of the Gongmao Steamboat Bureau, which sails between Suzhou and Dongshan, was robbed at Huangyang Bay at 4 pm on the 9th of this month, which has been published in various newspapers. Now, the bureau has submitted to the Su-Song Water Bandit Suppression Command, Commander Shen Baoyi's approval to open the case. Since the establishment of this headquarters, it has repeatedly ordered all districts to strictly abide by the regulations on suppressing bandits and protecting navigation. Now that the bandits dare to combine again during this winter defense period, harassing and intercepting merchant ships and endangering travelers, it is really disrespectful to the law. According to the report from the Second District in charge, an urgent order has been sent to speed up the supervision of the removal, tracking and suppression, and to rescue the captured passengers from danger. Now, according to the previous situation, it is strictly ordered to the Undertaking District Team to tighten the search and suppression, and to set a time limit for solving the case. It is also distributed to all district teams to conscientiously search for and rescue. Knowing this approval. And according to the Jiangsu Water Provincial Public Security Team, Second District, No. 137, it has been ordered to send fleet ships to encircle and suppress and rescue separately. Knowing this approval, etc. to the bureau. With such strict suppression by the Department District, it will not be difficult to solve the case soon.

Taicang

Water and Land Police Teams Search and Arrest Citizens

At about 9 pm on the 13th of this month, a special curfew was suddenly imposed in the city. The water public security team and the county public security bureau's plainclothes team patrolled the city gates strictly, with double posts guarding them, and conducted strict searches. The residents were extremely panicked, and did not know why the citizens Wang Yue and Lu Zhongtao were arrested. This morning, they were escorted to the Suzhou Bandit Suppression Department by the water public security team. What crimes the two committed have not yet been announced. All sectors are now discussing rescue methods.

As the Weather Gets Colder and the Year Ends, Bandits Are Rampant

Near Penglai Town in the county, at about 10 pm on the 13th, a bandit ship suddenly arrived in the Jiagou River, with more than 30 bandits on board, intending to rob. A villager happened to pass by and saw that their behavior was suspicious, so he immediately reported to the town police, who, together with the Dongqiao Security Corps, surrounded and arrested them. After a fierce battle of about an hour, the bandits were defeated and fled to the northwest. Also, at the homes of Zhou Pin and Erjia in Xintang City, at about 9 pm on the same evening, more than ten bandits suddenly came, broke through the gate, and robbed all the valuable clothes and ornaments, causing a loss of about five or six hundred yuan. In addition, at Bailong Temple outside the North Gate, three people wearing cotton robes and short clothes suddenly arrived last night. The abbot Ren Hong saw that their behavior was suspicious and quickly escaped from the back door, reporting to the police on duty and nearby residents to surround and arrest them. One bandit was captured on the spot, and handcuffs were found on him. The other two bandits escaped without a trace. The witnesses were all sent to the County Public Security Bureau for questioning. They confessed to intending to rob and were immediately detained.

Wuxi

Bloody Tragedy, the Culprit Escorted to the Court

Zhang Jiliang, the machine operator of the Guangming Theater in front of the City Library, was gathered and violently beaten by Xu Lao Er, Xue Linbao, Zhu Yaokui, etc. of the Xinguang Theater on the evening of the 10th of this month, smashing Jiliang's head. He was immediately sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment and has been there for five days. His condition is critical and he has been in a coma all day, urinating all over the bed. Yesterday, he was re-consulted by Western doctor Zhu Daozhou, who said that he needed to have his skull cut open to remove the broken bones, which might be able to save him. The culprit Xue Linbao was escorted to the County Court by the Public Security Bureau yesterday for investigation and detention. Xu Lao Er and others have been sought by Wu Xing'er, the manager of Xinguang, to be handed over to the case and dealt with.

Sheep Tip Town Smashes a Poison Pill Organization

The chief police officer of the Sixteenth Branch of the Anzhen Public Security Bureau in the Eighth District of the county recently arrested an old woman in this town who was selling red pills. The bureau chief Xunwei ordered her to say that the old woman's red pills came from Lu Bingzhong in Yangzhen. The branch chief immediately ordered them to go to search and arrest Lu Zilin and his partner Li Zhengyang, and seized 47,750 black pills, half a bag of raw materials for red pills, weighing 23 and a half catties, and a pill-making machine, as well as account books of various past customers and photos of Lu Bingzhong. He immediately temporarily detained them at the bureau and transferred them to the city yesterday to be sent to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Guangdong Education Inspection Group Arrives in Wuxi

The Guangzhou Education Inspection Group of the Ministry of Education of the Republic of China is going to various places in the country this time to inspect the situation of school education and social education, and to collect educational historical materials from all parties in preparation for holding a Guangzhou exhibition from February 15 to March 15 next year. The group departed from Guangzhou on the 11th of this month and passed through Xiamen, Shanghai, Nanjing, Tianjin, Jinan, and Beiping. The group arrived in Wuxi from Zhenjiang the night before, a total of five people. Yesterday morning, the group's supervisors Zhou Jiequan and Hu Boxiao went to the local education bureau to discuss matters. The bureau chief and Zhang Xiangsen, Hua Jinji, etc. received them and decided to visit the local primary and secondary schools and social education institutions today, and the county chamber of commerce will introduce them to visit the factory.

Changzhou

The Exposure of Forged Gold Bracelets in Pawn Shops

The Xincheng Pawn Shop in Beizhi Street, Wuyi, cracked down on a criminal named Xi Jianlin who pawned fake gold bracelets. The witness was sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Then, Hengchun, Jiheng, and Deyuan Erdian also sent representatives who had also been defrauded of fake gold bracelets to the Public Security Bureau to confront the criminal. The Public Security Bureau considered the case to be serious and transferred the criminal to the County Court for prosecution and interrogation. Unexpectedly, within four days, Jiang Maoren and Zhao Xinyuan's two silver shops also exchanged three pairs of fake gold bracelets. It is said that the official office has captured the criminals in this case, and they immediately filed a complaint for investigation and treatment, saying that they should be investigated and dealt with severely.

Dao Sheng Gang Members Sent to Martial Law Headquarters

The Sheng Qianzhuang money shop in West Wood Street of this city was robbed of over two thousand yuan in cash and foreign currency last month. After investigation by the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, they obtained clues a few days ago and arrested five principal offenders, Mou Changrong, Zhang Tianzhi, Lu Rongfu, Chen Yutian, and Wei Yuting, at Zhongshan Bridge. The team leader Shao Hanzhang then escorted them to the General Bureau on the morning of the [blank]th. It was also revealed that two accomplices, Shen Xingwen and Zhao Maozhi, were still at large. Nantong

Defense Expenditure Assessment Finalized

The Nantong County defense expenditure has been determined to be 240,000 yuan per year after several meetings among all sectors. The provincial government reduced this to 168,000 yuan. The assessment quota has now been allocated. The agricultural sector will be assessed 2.43 yuan per mu of land. The commercial sector will be assessed 49,300 yuan. The remaining 5,000 yuan will be compensated by special donations from overseas residents.

Pig Boat Capsizes Outside Wolf Mountain Port

A pig merchant surnamed Wu from Xin'gang Town was transporting more than fifty pigs to Shanghai. On the night of the 13th, the boat capsized in a storm on the river outside Wolf Mountain Port. Wu was rescued by the water police and survived, but eight of his companions are missing, and the pigs drowned and were lost.

Ningbo

Devastating Fire in Zhenbei Burns Entire Village

Wu Lu Village in Zhenbei, with more than eighty households, mostly farmers, unexpectedly caught fire in Hou Xinwu on the morning of the 12th at 11:00 AM. The fire spread rapidly due to a strong northwest wind. Although firefighters rushed to the scene to extinguish the blaze, their efforts were futile due to the intensity of the wind and fire. The fire burned for four hours before being extinguished. More than 130 of the village's 150 houses were destroyed. Only six or seven families, including Wang Caisheng and Wu Heshen, were spared. The rest were reduced to ashes. The total loss is estimated at around 100,000 yuan. More than one hundred villagers, old and young, are now homeless and hungry, urgently in need of relief. During the fire, a woman named A'xiu saw the fire spreading to her house. Her young son was sick in bed, and she rushed inside to rescue him but was unable to escape before a wall collapsed, burying them both in the fire.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Issues Declaration on the Restoration of Sino-Russian Diplomatic Relations

Soviet Russia's Mass Production

Will Forever Be Developed in the Far East

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a declaration yesterday on the restoration of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations, stating: "Sino-Russian trade began in the early years of the Kangxi Emperor and has a history of more than two hundred years. Moreover, the two countries share a border, and hundreds of thousands of Chinese people reside in Russia in the northeastern and northwestern provinces. Russian land trade has extended its reach throughout the Tian Shan Mountains, both north and south, and Mongolia. The complexity of the relationship and the length of history are unparalleled globally. In recent years, although diplomatic relations have been stagnant, Soviet Russian commerce has continued to advance rapidly, from Harbin in the north to Shanghai in the south, demonstrating that human-made obstacles cannot overcome natural advantages. China and Soviet Russia, in general, are both industrially backward countries. However, Soviet Russia has recently achieved success with its Five-Year Plan, and its heavy industry has jumped to the forefront. Our country, mired in production decline and economic depression, is unfortunately facing aggression by a powerful enemy and the loss of its borders. We should learn from our neighbors and actively build so as to defend the border and resist foreign insults. Wang Xiaolai, chairman of this chamber, proposed the restoration of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations at the National Crisis Conference convened by the National Government in Luoyang in April of this year. This wish has been realized today. Therefore, this restoration of diplomatic relations and exchange of ambassadors between China and Russia is a measure that the government should take and a common practice in international relations. We hope that the people of both countries, in light of the long history and the border relationship, can form a sincere, frank, and permanent union, so as not to betray this innate situation. Soviet Russia's mass production will forever be developed in the Far East market and sincerely accepted by the 400 million people. Furthermore, the Chinese people are rich in the nature of peace and patience, and their national policy seeks only to obtain freedom and equality as the greatest wish. The struggles over the years have been purely peaceful and legal. Conspiracy and intrigue are deeply despised by China, and repaying evil with virtue is not allowed by the sages. As the situation in the Far East becomes increasingly bleak, all friendly countries that uphold justice, regardless of their history, political situation, or status, will be regarded as the good people of the 400 million people and given the greatest commercial convenience. Putting stones on someone who has fallen into a well is a public enemy of human mutual aid. Chinese citizens, in order to uphold human morality, should not be indiscriminate. All friendly countries should take note of this."

Russian Residents Express Joy After the Restoration of Sino-Russian Diplomatic Relations

There are Approximately 15,000 Russian Residents in Shanghai

The Russian Consulate General in Shanghai Will Soon Be Restored

........................................................................................

The Candidates for Ambassadors from Both Sides May Be Announced Soon

Sino-Russian diplomatic relations have been severed since 1927, a period of five years. During these five years, there has been no clear investigation of the status of Russian residents in China and other matters between the two countries. Now that Sino-Russian diplomatic relations have been restored, the two countries will become closer in the future, and a preliminary investigation is very important. A reporter from the Central News Agency went to various Russian institutions in Shanghai yesterday to inquire about the details, which are recorded below.

Number of Russian Residents in Shanghai

Since the severance of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations and the withdrawal of ambassadors and consuls from both sides, there has been no overall statistics on the number of Russian residents in China. Therefore, the exact number of Russian residents in Shanghai is temporarily impossible to investigate. According to Russian Association personnel yesterday, there are many White Russians in Shanghai, and about 15,000 have registered with the association. There are about 500 Red Russians in Shanghai. The number of Russians in Shanghai is already large, and in order to seek contact and friendship, there are organizations like the United Association of Russian Institutions in Shanghai, the Russian Association, the Chamber of Commerce, the Merchant Ship Association, the Relief Association, the United Association of Disabled Veterans, the Performing Arts Association, and the Russian Merchants Assistance Association. There is only one Russian school, located on Dumei Road.

Russian Consulate to be Restored

The former site of the Russian Consulate General in Shanghai is at No. 1 Huangpu Beach Road, a magnificent building. Since 1927, it has only had one Indian guard, and the scene is quite desolate. According to representatives from the Russian business community yesterday, personnel will be sent to repair it within days for use after the restoration of the consulate. The Russian embassy will be located in Nanjing to facilitate contact with all affairs. Russian consulates in other places such as Beiping, Tianjin, Hankou, Jiujiang, Guangzhou, and Fuzhou will also be restored in order. In places with fewer Russian residents, commercial offices will be established first.

Candidates for Ambassadors from Both Sides

Regarding the selection of ambassadors from both sides, the reporter inquired of a certain source from the Russian side yesterday. It was said that the candidate for the Soviet Russian ambassador to China could not be decided before the announcement. However, according to information obtained by this person, the current president of Moscow University, Lautik, and the former ambassador to China, Karakhan, have the highest calls. It is said that the Soviet people are very happy about the restoration of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations. It is said that the candidate for our country's ambassador to Russia has already been internally decided to be Yan Huiquing, the current minister to the United States.

Russian Merchants Express Joy

In order to understand the current status of Russian commerce in China, the reporter drove to visit Lai Wen, the manager of the Russian Merchants Assistance Association. According to him, Russian commerce has suffered great losses since the severance of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations in 1927, which has now lasted for five years. At the beginning of the severance of diplomatic relations, Russian merchants going to Hankou were sometimes detained by local military police on suspicion. Now that the restoration of diplomatic relations has been announced, the above-mentioned pain can be completely eliminated, and the Chinese and Russian people can now join hands in the Far East. The transportation of Russian goods to China has always been loaded and shipped abroad, which is very inconvenient. Today's urgent task is to restore navigation between the two countries.

The Latest Invention: Microlight Wireless Telephone

The World's Shortest Radio Waves

The Number of Vibrations per Second

Can Reach 200 Million Times

Scientific progress is changing with each passing day. The wireless telephone on the Italian wheel, which can transmit language as if conversing in the same room over tens of thousands of miles between Shanghai and Rome, has caused astonishment among Chinese people. However, this ordinary wireless telephone has become an old thing in today's scientific world. The latest invention is a wireless telephone that transmits with micro-light, and its wavelength can be shortened to less than one foot. This short-wave telephone was first put into practical use about eighteen months ago. The International Telegraph and Telephone Company, in its laboratory in London, England, and the laboratory of the Paris Telephone Materials Company, jointly installed it between the English and French Channels. Its wavelength is only 7.1 inches, which is a new invention in the electrical world. Yesterday, according to the Shanghai Telephone Company, the International Telegraph and Telephone Company telegraphed that the British Aviation Department had ordered the latest micro-light wireless radio from the Standard Telephone and Cable Company, a branch of the company in England. The wavelength has been shortened to 5.9 inches, which can be said to be the world's shortest wave. It will be installed at the British Lemn Airfield, and the French Aviation Department will also install the same radio at the Saint-Ingler-Faner Airfield to report on aircraft crossing the English Channel to each other. It is expected to be launched next spring.

According to this kind of short-wave radio, the transmitting and receiving antenna is less than one inch long. When generating electricity, a special micro-tube is used to generate vibrations that are sufficient to generate micro-light. The number of vibrations can reach 200 million times per second. This very rapid vibration is transmitted through the transmitting antenna, concentrated into a micro-beam by a set of mirrors, and sent to the sky by a circular reflecting mirror with a diameter of about ten feet to reach the same reflecting mirror of the receiving radio. The ones ordered by the British Aviation Department this time are also equipped with an electric printer at both ends, so that even if the receiving staff is temporarily away, the telegram can be automatically printed and stored. The advantages of micro-light wireless radio are: 1. It is almost completely unaffected by the weather; 2. Because the radio waves are very short, it can actually be free from the interference of nearby machines or radio waves.
