Free Talk

Their Road (II)

— By 药影H.Barbusse

No matter how the fire started, it quickly and thoroughly devoured the entire house. It concealed everything inside. The efficiency of the buckets was only enough to cool the charred ends of the beams when the roof frame collapsed. Everyone piled the remnants on both sides of the road; in the ashes, only the iron bed frame still retained its human form...

But when the fire broke out, no one bothered to inform the residents of the burned house in Tuolang, nor did anyone notify them afterward.

"They'll find out soon enough," a gossipy woman blurted out.

"Yes," Old Remy echoed with a stifled and monotonous voice, sounding the truth.

As evening approached, bringing back the victims, a sense of emotion filled the village. Many faces, driven by curiosity and fear, peeked out from the dark doorways. Then, everyone gathered in the square, crowded so tightly that not even a messenger could pass... All eyes were fixed on the sky, on the hilltop, like a group of prisoners gathered in the darkness, waiting for a shooting star to appear.

"Look, they're over there!" Gaspar hissed quietly.

"It's impossible!" Two women, overwhelmed by fear, exclaimed in unison.

In the distance, on the red hills, they appeared together. Suddenly, everyone realized they were unaware of their disaster. They were still walking towards that vast open space, the space where their burned house once stood, with their usual calm steps.

The onlookers standing below became restless. The condemned couple, though walking towards the punishment prepared for them by fate, were still talking, and despite being so close, they saw nothing. Their minds were entirely focused on each other; they had become detached from the world.

They drew nearer… nearer… Suddenly, they raised their heads, looking ahead…

"Ah!" A beggar, allowed to participate in this event for the sake of charity, sighed.

But even then, they still saw nothing. Undoubtedly, their thoughts, like their face-to-face conversation, were completely concentrated on each other… They smiled with exactly the same smile. Could anyone see or guess at this smile? "That adds a beautiful, pitiful, dim vortex to the human face?" Whether visible or not, everyone thought so.

After a while, the man and woman carelessly passed between the two piles of burned debris: they continued walking, unable to recognize what lay at their feet; they disappeared on the other side, on the side where the sun rises.

The faces of the onlookers showed horror and bewilderment, as they speculated in the dim light.

Even though Aiete, the woman, had a stomach full of words, these words were too simple for her to express; she only moved her lips. But as soon as she did, old Remy calmly responded with a "Yes"...

…Yes… Yes… Everyone thought so. Yes, obviously… They were "elsewhere," so they saw nothing… Yes, their road stretched out clearly before them, they continued walking, and that was it. Yes, they were not stopped by their house; that was only natural, because their house was no longer there…

Note: The author, Henri Barbusse, is a world-renowned writer like Romain Rolland. Born in 1873, he began his literary activities in his youth, with poetry collections such as "The Weepers" (Ｐleureuses) and novels such as "Hell" (Enfer). However, it was not until the publication of his novel "Fire" (Lefeu) during the European War, which depicted the horrors of war, that he occupied an important position in the world literary scene. This piece is translated from his earliest collection of short stories, "We Others" (Nousartre).

"Gambling" Education

— By 星子

In yesterday's newspaper, there were two reports about "gambling." One was about a cook who committed theft and was imprisoned for gambling on lottery tickets. In prison, he still muttered the names of lottery tickets such as "Wang Zhigao" and "Li Yuebao," and frequently asked people what the lottery numbers were for the day. The other was about a rickshaw puller who pawned his rickshaw and his wife's laundry for a final gamble, ultimately losing everything, resulting in the tragic deaths of the husband hanging himself and the wife poisoning herself. These two tragic scenes about "gambling" are common occurrences in Shanghai. But precisely because they have become "common occurrences" that are ignored by the general public, we feel that these "common occurrences" contain extremely serious social implications.

Originally, the backwardness of education in our country is undeniable. However, the education about "gambling" is extremely developed, and its design and teaching methods are extremely persuasive. Taking Shanghai as an example, when a child in Shanghai reaches the age of six or seven, there are often street vendors selling sweets waiting for him at the entrance of the alley. Mothers can take their children at any time to learn the preliminary knowledge of gambling and tell them how to win a piece of candy with a smile. As the child grows older, to nine or ten years old, this kind of infantile education is naturally no longer appropriate. Therefore, there are already stalls for dice games at the entrance of the alley waiting. The child can also ask his mother for a few copper coins at any time to experience the taste of drinking and gambling. If the father and mother entertain guests with mahjong, then the child can further gain a very correct concept and interest in gambling from the factual lessons of his father and mother. When the child grows a little older, on the roads around the Great World and Dongxin Bridge, there are friends wearing short clothes waving various gambling tools in their hands to beckon people, and every game field is also equipped with special seats for gambling, where you can try your luck at any time. As for adults, there are even more specialized schools about gambling, including racetracks, dog racing tracks, jai alai, and roulette casinos. The City God Temple is filled with mahjong tiles and dominoes, and small cigarette paper shops are frequently plastered with lottery tickets. The magic hand of "chance" firmly grips everyone, and as soon as you slip, you can be thrown into the tragic deep pit of "husband hanging himself, wife poisoning herself."

If this kind of "gambling education" is allowed to develop in this way, then the tragedies of "hanging oneself and poisoning oneself" will forever be regarded as "common occurrences." However, is this really a "common occurrence"?

Winter Suburbs

— By 司晨

In the suburbs, one side of the pond bank is fields, and the other side is water. The water is so low that the sails of the boats moving along are level with the bank. The fields are so scattered, with puddles and irregular mounds of graves interspersed among them.

It's just past the halfway point of the afternoon, and the sun is already hurrying westward. And it's hurrying so quickly, as we can see from the gradual lengthening of the shadows of the passing boat sails.

With the wind, the sails are raised, and one or two people tow the boat with a rope. Those on the boat can do other chores in the sunlight. Those on the shore can also feel quite comfortable walking on the soft, wool-like withered grass.

Seeing these spreading, weak wild grasses that have come all the way from the fields to the pond bank, one feels a childlike curiosity. There's nothing much in the fields, so let's set a fire and burn them. It really catches fire, so quickly. The flames don't look very big in the sunlight, but the white smoke billows high enough.

The water chestnut fields have turned into puddles, and some remaining trunks lie askew. Someone is feeling for snails in another larger puddle. Still others are hunched over, digging for water chestnuts in the muddy fields.

There is one very large puddle, perhaps we can call it a swamp, with flocks of ducks swimming in the water, probing their heads into the water to find food. The scene is very lively. Suddenly, the duck herder calls out loudly from the edge of the field, and the ducks start to call out loudly as if they had received an order. There must be more than five hundred of them. They climb onto the field ridge while calling out. It's so interesting to see them crowding together so tightly when they eat!

Gradually, night is approaching. The sun suddenly sinks below the horizon, and only a few piles of red clouds remain on the horizon. The pale image of the cold moon has been carved into the sky, and the evening crows are cawing as they search for their old homes in the twilight.

Discussion on "Conditions for Love"

— Zhong Jie

"Love has conditions," this is a principle that no one can deny. Otherwise, everyone could love anyone, everyone would be lovable, which would simply be equivalent to the promiscuity of primitive times, and there would be no "love" to speak of!

But what are the conditions for love? That is, what is the standard for love? Regarding this question, Ms. Wei Ji already provided an answer in a discussion on the 13th of this month. The standards she proposed were profound knowledge, noble morality, shared thoughts, upward aspirations, strong willpower, special talents, strong physique, considerable age, and gentle temperament. As for money and beauty, Ms. Wei Ji believes that they are base and vulgar and should not be included as conditions. It is very obvious that Ms. Wei Ji's view is not very correct, because if all 1.6 billion people in the world were to choose a spouse according to Ms. Wei Ji's conditions, then at least 1.5 billion people would never find their match!

We believe that there are only two words for the conditions of love, that is, "suitable" or "fitting". Whether in terms of material or spiritual aspects, external or internal qualities, it must be, and only needs to be, "mutually suitable". Whether it is knowledge, talent, temperament, physique, age... as well as the wealth and appearance that Ms. Wei Ji considers base, they must also be suitable. Of course, the "suitability" mentioned here will never be "absolutely suitable", but only "suitably suitable". If all conditions are "suitable", and there is still a slight difference in one condition, then I think it is also fine, because we believe that nothing in the world is "perfect" or "completely good."

Property, of course, should also be listed as one of the conditions. We don't need to "overcorrect"; nor can we leave reality and engage in empty talk. In a capitalist society, before it collapses, no one can transcend the power of money. No matter how you say it, love is pure, great, and beyond everything, but the material environment of society actually dominates all human actions and thoughts. The philosopher Karl once said: "The material environment of society dominates human consciousness; it is not human consciousness that dominates the material environment of society." Love should also stand on a materialist standpoint and should not seek a basis in stale idealism.

But we are not advocating that "the richer the property, the more it meets our ideal conditions." We only advocate "suitability". In short: we advocate that everything has a balanced suitability, talent, knowledge, insight, thought, ambition, age, wealth, and appearance can all be suitable. This is the real condition for love.

If Ms. Wei Ji is a woman with profound knowledge, noble morality, strong willpower, special talents, and gentle temperament, then I fully agree with her opinion, because such a perfect woman should have a man with corresponding conditions as a partner. If Ms. Wei Ji is not as I imagined in my ideal, then she would be "demanding of others with Zhou's strictness and lenient with oneself"! However, this is not within the scope of the question.

Long Novel

The Crossroads of the Times and Love Sixteen

— Zhang Ziping

Perhaps it was because he had drunk one too many cups of coffee in the Russian restaurant, Haiquan lay in bed and couldn't fall asleep no matter what. After a while, he heard a burst of laughter from downstairs.

'Could those Japanese devils be laughing at me?'

So he became even more resentful of Mrs. Tsuruko.

When he woke up, there seemed to be some sunlight coming through the window. He raised himself up halfway and looked outside. Sure enough, the sky was very clear this morning. He quickly got up, put on his clothes, and went down to the second floor, intending to go to the bathroom to wash up. But when he reached the bathroom door, he saw that the door was tightly closed from the inside.

'Who is it?'

His voice was a bit sharp. But there was no reply from inside. After a while, he suddenly heard a series of coughing sounds from inside.

'Who is it?'

His voice was even louder. At the same time, he thought, this is really outrageous. Could it be that Mr. Zeng came back last night?

'Excuse me, Mr. Lin, please wait a moment. I'm really sorry.'

Mrs. Tsuruko, still wearing her pajamas, stretched her upper body out from her bedroom, rubbing her eyes and nodding to him with a smile. Her voice was even softer than usual, and her attitude was as if to say, 'This is unavoidable, please forgive me this time.'

He thought, could it be that she really dared to leave that Japanese man to stay in this house last night? If that were the case, then that would be truly outrageous! He was about to question her when he suddenly saw a young girl standing behind Mrs. Tsuruko, wearing a Japanese-style dress, with her hair draped over her shoulders. A pair of pure black pupils stared intently at Haiquan. He had never seen such a beautiful girl. The girl's complexion was so white, like the mid-autumn moon. Her attire was also very fashionable, like a cloud of colorful clouds. Haiquan was dazzled and speechless for a moment. Glancing at the beautiful Japanese girl, he quickly suppressed the angry expression on his face, put on a serious expression, and went back up to the third floor.

He sorted out the books he would use today and then planned to go downstairs to the bathroom to relieve himself. As soon as he stepped out of the room, he saw a bald Japanese man, about fifty years old, walking up the stairs step by step, wearing a kimono, a Japanese-style robe. Haiquan recognized that it was the Japanese clothing that Mr. Zeng often wore at home. How could this Japanese man be so bold, acting as the owner of this house? He really wanted to go forward and punch him. But he was afraid of causing trouble, so he had to endure it. He saw that when the Japanese man reached his door, he bowed to him very humbly. This attitude moved Haiquan. Haiquan also quickly returned a bow.

After washing up, when he returned to his room, he saw a porcelain plate on his table with four slices of toast and a cup of hot milk. In the past, Mrs. Tsuruko would accompany him to breakfast every morning. Why did she specially send his portion here today? He couldn't figure out the reason and was feeling unhappy.

Expectation

— Lu Wei

It's dusk, and the mist is hazy.

I walked out of the West Gate alone, crossed a street full of cow dung and pig dung, and with light steps and a melancholy mood, I soon arrived in the maple forest.

The maple forest was full of blood-red maple leaves, and the evening breeze blew gently, making a rustling sound. All the crops in the fields have been harvested. I sat down on a stone. My expectant mood was very urgent. I had made an appointment with him, and he was coming to the maple forest at dusk. I was waiting for him.

Slowly, many stories of my childhood playing in this maple forest were evoked in my memory. The friends who played with me at that time are now scattered. Because of the oppression of life, who can permanently hold on to the joy and carefree mood of youth? I often sit alone in the maple forest and think, and sadness always surrounds my heart.

This evening, I made an appointment with him to come to this maple forest to see me. I don't know if he can come, but how much I miss him! I hope he comes, I have something to say to him.

The sky gradually darkened, and the shadows in the maple forest gradually expanded.

My heart became bitter, he's not coming! I thought like this.

The sky is dark. I have to go home. I can't wait any longer. I sighed in disappointment, picked up a red maple leaf, and wrote on it with a steel pen: "This is a drifting heart." I took it home.

When I got home, my mother asked me earnestly:

"Where have you been? We were so worried waiting for you!"

I had nothing to say. I only ate half a bowl of rice for dinner and felt like I was going to vomit something.

Fighting

— Wu

Speaking of fighting, friends like A Q will definitely stick out their tongues, from which it can be seen that fighting is not a fun thing, but there are also people like Li Kui, who are full of energy when fighting is mentioned. Such people will inevitably damage the gentleman's style. A "gentleman" is "a person who is gentle and refined," and everyone is willing to be a gentleman, so everyone has to reluctantly put on a gentle and refined appearance.

China has few people like Li Kui, but many people like A Q, so China is still a country of gentlemen. However, people like A Q are not completely useless. When you are preparing to beat him, he can be magnanimous and indifferent. Even if you spit in his face, he will smile and wipe it off with his sleeve, and apologize to you. But if you are still unwilling and actually give him two slaps on the face, then he has no choice but to scold you, "Damn it," and quickly step back three steps, touch his face; but he will still say with a smiling face: "Gentlemen use words, villains use fists. Why did you hit someone?" Of course, he is much better than you, because he is actually a gentleman. Afterwards, if you are still willing to be a villain, rush forward, full of murderous intent, and must beat him so that he can't get up from the ground, at this time, he seems to really have no way to endure it, immediately retreat three steps again, scold from your mother all the way to three generations of ancestors, roll up his sleeves, pull up his heels, and seem to immediately aim his head at your chest. But the enemy is still coming fiercely, and the situation is obviously not very good; so he immediately realizes that "a brave man does not suffer immediate losses," and changes his mind, preparing for "long-term resistance," and shouts loudly with all his strength: "I'm not fighting you now, wait for me tomorrow!" In this way, he runs away without a trace.

Therefore, China will not perish, because there are indeed many such people.

The Measurement of the Depth of the Sea

— Jing

Everyone knows that in order to ensure the safety of navigation, the depth of the sea must be measured precisely.

In the past, the simple measurement method was to use a long rope, with a hammer tied at the bottom, vertically into the sea. After the hammer touched the seabed, the length of the rope was calculated. This method is still used today. At the bottom of the hammer, a hollow hole is often carved, filled with animal oil, so that the soil quality of the seabed can be known by the shells or sand attached to the bottom of the hammer.

However, if the ocean is too deep, such as to thousands of meters, then the time when the hammer touches the seabed is not easy to know, and because the seawater pressure is too high, a large hammer must be used, and the rope must also be thick, so when it is pulled out of the water, the weight is increased due to the resistance of the water, which is indeed a very troublesome matter. Therefore, two types of electric depth sounders and echo sounders are now mostly used.

On the weight of the electric depth sounder, there is a thin glass tube two feet long, installed in a protective brass tube. The glass tube is coated with red Chromium silver acid. In proportion to the pressure of seawater, the part immersed in seawater will turn white, so by calculating the division of this white Chromium silver acid, the depth of the ocean can be known.

The echo sounder, in addition to the disadvantage of not knowing the soil quality of the seabed, can measure precisely and easily for weather and the speed of the ship. The principle is very simple, that is, from the time it takes for the sound waves emitted from the water surface to reach the seabed and then echo back to the water surface, the depth of the water can be known. The speed of sound waves in seawater is about 1,500 meters per second, then the deep sea of 10,000 meters can be measured in a few seconds.

Second Estimated Report on National Cotton Production in the 21st Year

(Decrease of 2,734,299 dan compared to the first estimate)

The China Cotton Statistics Association announced the second estimate of national cotton production for the 21st year at 5:00 PM on December 15th of the 21st year as follows:

(Cotton Field Area: 37,079,835 mu)

(Ginned Cotton Production: 8,094,863 dan)

The above estimates are based on reports from: 1) Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, Shaanxi, Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, eleven provinces, and the two municipalities of Tianjin and Shanghai; 2) The cotton crop conditions before December 10th; 3) The losses from disasters suffered by cotton crops in various provinces before December 10th have already been included; 4) Cotton fields are measured in mu, and cotton production is measured in dan.

The comparison of the two estimates for this year with the cotton field production of previous years is shown below:

|Year|Cotton Field Area|Ginned Cotton Production|

|---|---|---|

|8|33,037,881|9,028,390|

|9|28,307,290|6,750,403|

|10|28,216,168|5,429,220|

|11|33,464,595|8,310,355|

|12|29,554,053|7,144,642|

|13|28,771,577|7,808,882|

|14|28,121,027|7,534,351|

|15|27,349,727|6,243,585|

|16|27,610,276|6,722,108|

|17|31,926,311|8,839,274|

|18|33,811,255|7,587,021|

|19|37,593,012|8,809,567|

|20 First Estimate|35,468,352|8,793,241|

|Second Estimate|34,182,747|6,460,641|

|Final Revision|31,637,779|6,399,780|

|21 First Estimate|37,086,775|10,829,162|

|Second Estimate|37,079,835|8,094,863|

This year's cotton production, according to the Association's first estimate, reached 10,829,162 dan, the largest production in recent years. This was mainly because the Yellow River basin, which is prone to drought, received sufficient rainfall this year, and the cotton fields developed extremely well. The yield per mu exceeded 100 jin. Although the south suffered from heavy rain and cold, conditions were generally good. Therefore, the national average yield was 30 jin of ginned cotton per mu (equivalent to 100 jin of seed cotton). The collection of 100 jin of cotton from 100 jin of seed cotton is only considered a normal harvest, and it is rare for the national average to achieve a normal harvest. After the first estimate was released, the climate in the cotton-growing areas gradually deteriorated, contrary to the past. In the north, rainfall went from appropriate to excessive, and river water overflowed. Many cotton fields in Hebei, Shandong, and Shanxi were flooded, and early frost further damaged the cotton harvest. At that time, the south was experiencing drought. This phenomenon already existed during the first estimate. Rainfall remained scarce in August and September. Autumn typhoons, which are common in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, fortunately did not occur this year, but the drought caused boll shedding, which also had a significant impact on the cotton harvest. Therefore, before the first estimate in August, the weather conditions in the cotton-growing areas of both the north and south were good, but after the estimate, the situation changed to the opposite, leading to a gradual decline in the expected normal cotton harvest, especially in Hubei, Shandong, and Henan provinces. Hubei was also facing bandit suppression, which had a considerable impact. The only province with relatively good conditions was Jiangsu, but the increase was minimal. Overall, the second estimate was significantly lower than the first estimate. Hubei decreased by two-fifths, and Shandong decreased by one-third. Jiangsu was the only province with an increase, but the increase was very small. The overall national cotton production decreased by 2,734,299 dan compared to the first estimate, a decrease of 25%. The quality also slightly deteriorated. Due to the heavy rainfall in the north during the peak boll-forming period, the cotton production in the northern provinces, which rarely had yellow stains, greatly increased this year. Shandong and Hebei experienced particularly early frost, and "frost yellow," which is commonly referred to in the cotton industry, was also prevalent. In the south, the prolonged drought and scarce rainfall during the boll-opening period prevented the cotton fruits from developing fully, and there were also quite a few immature fibers. Therefore, the quality of national cotton production was also inferior. (The rest is omitted)

Grains

Rice Market Eases with Clear Weather

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, goods arrived from the Yangtze River, numbering in the thirties and forties, but sales in this street were sluggish. Thick japonica rice prices weakened due to news from Changzhou and Wuxi that market prices were softening, and the price was cheaper than that of Shenhua rice. However, Kunshan rice remained stable. Buyers saw a surge in goods and poor sales, and opening prices decreased by 0.2 yuan. Late rice purchases by brokers neared 1,000 dan, and prices were similar to the previous day. The supply of Du Yang tip rice also decreased, and transactions suddenly slowed, with prices fluctuating slightly. There was still a large supply of early rice, but there were no transactions, and prices were at 0.2 yuan. Rice from Suzhou and Tongxiang arrived steadily, and the market saw no fluctuations (Xinzha). Yesterday, more than 40 boats arrived. Transactions of country rice were the most common, and market conditions were stable. No one inquired about Changdai northern japonica rice and Kunshan rice. The price of Danyang Jiangyin rice had to fall. Sales of Zishan Qingjing early rice were particularly sluggish, with prices slightly below normal. Customer groups made few purchases of the Du tip rice, and prices remained stable. The price of Bianyin Yuan was dragged down slightly by the thick japonica rice.

Wuhu Machine Yuan Rice Suddenly Rises by 0.3 Yuan

(Speculators Purchase Rice from Jiangxi and Hunan)

Yesterday, the situation for customer sen rice was quite good, and the price of customer yuan rice especially showed improvement. Speculators inquired about customer sen rice, and the appetite was strong. The daily secret agreement has reached over 10,000 dan, and purchases were made in production areas such as Jiujiang. Areas such as Changsha, Hunan, Xiangpiao, and Yisuhe were particularly closely watched by speculators. It is said that the local rice industry has mostly been explored by customers in Shanghai and Nanjing. The amount has been estimated at 70,000 to 80,000 bags, so the local production price is high, and it will be difficult to transport from there in the future. Yesterday, speculators in this city also purchased 970 bags of Jiangxi machine rice, with prices ranging from 8.25 yuan to 8.35 yuan, which is 0.1 yuan higher than the previous day. Northern ocean rice is temporarily difficult to transport due to the difficulty in loading rice from the lower reaches of the river, and they also tried to purchase more than 100 bags of Hunan machine red rice in the market at a price of 8 yuan to 7.9 yuan. Recently, customer yuan rice has been thoroughly searched in the district, but it has not been successful. Yesterday, 400 bags of newly arrived Wuhu machine yuan rice were immediately purchased by the district gang, and the price suddenly rose by as much as 0.3 yuan, with prices ranging from 9.3 yuan, 9.25 yuan, to 9 yuan or more. In the future, customers and speculators all have intentions to facilitate purchases, and the market should be able to stabilize.

Strong Selling in the Distant-Month Flour Market

(Five More Ships of Han Wheat Scattered Warehouse Goods Are Agreed Upon)

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices of various months tended to stabilize again. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat was slightly lower by 0.1 jiao in Canada and higher by 4 or 5 cents in Chicago, the exchange rate was difficult to lower, and the outside market was mostly floating. Given the liveliness of the spot market, buying was very active. Although various factories had sales, they were still unable to satisfy demand, so the prices of various months were better by 7.5 li to 1 cent compared to the previous day. By the opening of the afternoon market, March had been urgently covering shorts, and the atmosphere was very good. Distant months also saw an increase due to the absorption of the Lian Gang. However, after 2 o'clock, they fell back again. A large batch of Australian warehouse goods was sold, totaling five ships, with a low price of 3.235 yuan. Gang Xin agreed to three ships, Fufeng agreed to one ship, and Xinda and others jointly agreed to one ship. Therefore, there were large-scale sales in various distant-month markets, and the quantity was substantial. However, the near-term market remained the same. The reason for this is that the near-term market is not active, and the distant-term market is difficult to sell. As a result, this month was down 0.25 li compared to the previous day, January was down 0.25 li, February was down 1.25 li, March was down 1.5 li, April was down 0.75 li, and May was down 1 li.

No Vitality in the Wheat Futures Market

After the opening of the wheat futures market yesterday morning and afternoon, the market generally showed a revolving image. With the quoted price of foreign wheat, there were few ups and downs. The selling side cannot be active without foreign wheat chips. The storage of local wheat in various places is really sparse, and the small amount of arrivals is conceivable. All sellers are not willing to say so if they do not have a real grasp, so trading is always sluggish and lifeless. Yesterday, only the first month was down by a small amount of 2 or 3 points at the beginning, and then rebounded. The remaining months had very few ups and downs. As a result, January was better by 1 point compared to the previous day, and the rest had no difference.

Sugar Market

New Tide Green Seen Looser in Later Market

(Coarse Sand White Sugar Withholding Not Yet Opened)

Yesterday's sugar market turned weaker due to the decline in the target price. The association plans to allocate and coarse sand white output households still call for 15.5 liang, and the input households get 15.4 liang, with a difference of one yuan, resulting in a withholding situation. 20th grade medium sand white goods are in short supply. The 18th grade medium white is 14.35 liang, which is five yuan less than the gang. The 80th and 90th grade Dutch red remain stable. A batch of new tide greens that arrived the other day has already been cleared for exchange yesterday, with a total of over 1,200 bags delivered. The price of Tizhuang green is still half a liang, followed by 9.4 yuan to 9.1 yuan, and then 8.9 yuan. There is a tendency for the market to weaken, because the new tide has just been found out, and there will inevitably be more goods arriving in the later period, and the number of points will inevitably fall. It is also expected.

Also, yesterday, I received overseas telecommunications, New York spot and December sugar prices unchanged. January, March, and May are slightly three pounds down, July and September are slightly one pound down, London December is slightly two and a half pence, March and May are slightly two and a quarter pence, and Java white sugar is unchanged and still sells for eight shillings and three pence.

Random Notes

Locomotive Starts Automatically

— Fo

According to reports yesterday, a strange event occurred on the Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway on the 4th of this month: a locomotive started automatically from Guangzhou towards Foshan without a driver. Some say that it was because the locomotive had too much firepower, and the steam hose on the engine was not tightly secured, and was forced open by the steam power, so it could start automatically without a driver. This is also a "presumptive" explanation, and may not necessarily be the case, because since the advent of trains, there has never been such a special situation.

Recently, strange and bizarre things in our country have been emerging one after another. Last year the Yellow River cleared, this year the Yellow River narrowed, and countless antiques and food were unearthed. Also, in some places, the "eye of heaven" opened, and in other places, monsters appeared. Although such events have been occasionally recorded in history, no one has ever witnessed them. Unexpectedly, recently these strange things have been seen quite often, so the automatic starting of a locomotive may also be one of the bizarre events. As the saying goes, "When the heavens rebel against the seasons, there will be disaster; when the earth rebels against its nature, there will be monsters; when people rebel against righteousness, there will be destitution." Given the current state of human affairs, why can't the mischievous creator play some tricks?

Moreover, the current world is a world of automatic driving. As long as you have enough firepower and enough power, you can charge straight ahead and drive automatically. For example, the Japanese disregard for public justice, tearing up alliances, forcibly occupying our three northeastern provinces, and opposing the League of Nations' mediation is the Japanese's automatic driving. With national crises looming and foreign disasters becoming increasingly urgent, instead of thinking about resisting foreign aggression, some ignore the orders of the central government, close their doors, and desperately engage in internal warfare. This is the warlords' automatic driving. Some engage in manipulative diplomacy, plotting and scheming, not caring about the people's suffering, not knowing that the country is about to perish, specializing in creating chaos, and not wanting to remedy the situation. This is the politicians' automatic driving. There are many examples of automatic driving, not just the locomotive on the Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway.

Chinese people not only drive automatically, but also like to drive in reverse. A car only has a forward path, and there is no reason to drive in reverse. However, Chinese people's cars often do not like to drive forward, but like to turn backward. So, no matter how much you change things, the result is that things get worse and worse. Rural areas are bankrupt, people are struggling to survive, and officials cannot provide relief, but instead add insult to injury, doing their best to exploit the people, cutting flesh to heal sores, causing even more harm. This is called driving in reverse. Soldiers are supposed to defend the country, and killing the enemy is their sacred duty, but our country's soldiers cannot defend the country and specialize in killing each other. This is called driving in reverse. Now, the cost of living in our country is increasing day by day, and livelihoods are becoming more and more difficult, but the modern society is desperately promoting extravagance and entertainment, which is also driving in reverse. Fortunately, the locomotive on the Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway, although it drove freely, did not go so far as to drive in reverse, which is good.

Furthermore, with regard to the Guangdong government, it seems to obey the orders of the central government, yet it also seems not to obey the orders of the central government. All matters of power and authority seem to be like the automatic driving of a locomotive, not completely bound by the orders of the central government. If human affairs can be driven automatically, why can't a locomotive be driven automatically?

Science

Method of Making Alcohol from Potatoes

— Chen Chongru

The method of making alcohol using potatoes as raw material is divided into four layers as follows:

The first layer is steaming:

Grind the starch of the potatoes into a paste. First, wash the potatoes clean, put them in a steamer, and steam them until they are very cooked. Roughly, the starch in the middle has all become gelatinized. Then take it out and mash it very finely and put it in a bucket.

The second layer is saccharification:

For starch to turn into sugar, it must first go through saccharification. Add malt to the cooked potatoes. This malt contains a kind of yeast that can turn gelatinized starch into sugar. So, when adding the malt, stir it very evenly. After stirring, wrap the bucket with rice straw so that the temperature in the bucket is often at 63 degrees Celsius on the thermometer. Saccharification is easiest at this temperature. In about four or five hours, the starch will all turn into sugar.

The third layer is fermentation:

Fermentation is turning sugar into alcohol. At that time, the temperature should be low, often between 13 degrees Celsius on the thermometer. Then add a kind of yeast and stir it evenly. After seven or eight hours, when the sugar turns into alcohol, the temperature is easy to rise. In these days, pay close attention.

The fourth layer is distillation:

The sugar solution that has been fermented still has many impurities in the middle. To extract alcohol, you must use distillation to slowly extract it. One distillation is not very pure. It must be distilled several times to become all alcohol. Alcohol has a wide range of uses, such as in the manufacture of perfume, floral water, and medicinal solutions, which are indispensable.

Tomorrow is the Due Date

— Sun Yuan

The class bell has rung for half an hour, but Professor W hasn't arrived yet. The classroom has turned into a talk shop, with everyone talking and laughing, talking about women and movies. This noise has reached the ears of the X Registrar in the office, but he doesn't dare to say a word, or even take a look, because he knows that if he steps into the classroom, he will immediately be questioned by the students until he is speechless. It's better to be "sensible" and turn a deaf ear.

Suddenly, several students spotted Professor W! How come they didn't hear his leather shoes? Actually, with such a racket, how could they hear him?

The talking and laughing gradually quieted down. Everyone took out their Conklin or Parker fountain pens, opened their notebooks, and straightened themselves up, posing as if they were about to write thousands of words. At the same time, dozens of pairs of eyes were staring at Professor W, as if they didn't recognize him, or as if they were trying to find some fault on his face, waiting quietly. Of course, there were also several pairs of eyes that were exceptions, focusing on something else.

Professor W's movements seemed much slower today. He slowly opened his black leather bag, slowly reached in, and slowly took out...

Ah! It wasn't a book, nor lecture notes, but a stack of white paper.

Ah! Another exam, annoying exam.

"Life-or-death exam," a female student whispered. "Today is the monthly exam," Professor W said, as if others didn't understand that there was to be an

Page 20

exam, specially explaining it. At the same time, he raised the stack of white paper, as if to prove that he wasn't lying. Then, he turned his back and wrote the exam questions on the blackboard.

"Professor W, we just had an exam last week, why are we having another one?"

"The regulations here state that there must be a monthly exam once a month. We are almost three months late, we only had one exam, so we must have one today."

"Professor W, you didn't notify us last week, we didn't prepare, how can we take the exam?"

"It doesn't matter, just write whatever you want. I was originally opposed to exams, but the registrar's office wants the grade sheets," Professor W said with a smile.

"If we can't pass, we won't take the exam!"

"No exam!"

"No exam!"

"Hey! Hey! Don't worry, just write whatever you want. This doesn't count as an exam, just consider it that I'm asking you to write an essay!" Because the "no exam" cries were too loud, Professor W raised his voice and said "Hey, hey" several times, but he was still smiling.

"If it's being graded, isn't it an exam? Haha!"

"Haha."

"Professor W, let's take it home to do, and hand it in to you next week."

"Hey! Just write whatever you want, why take it home to do?"

"Professor W, it's getting late, let's just go back!"

"Hey! Hey! Just write whatever you want in class, no need to take it back to do," Professor W finally said with a smile.

"Then, we'll just hand it in to you tomorrow!"

"Hey! Hey! Just write whatever you want!" He was still smiling.

Professor W finally walked down the podium and distributed the white paper one by one to the students. Some students in the front rows refused to receive it, but after Professor W explained, "Whether you take it home to do, or do it in class, you'll still need the paper!" they finally accepted it.

"Now, please everyone start writing." He said.

"Ding ding..." The end-of-class bell rang.

"Then we'll hand it in tomorrow!"

The sound of leather shoes disappeared as Professor W disappeared at the classroom door, followed by a burst of loud laughter, which replaced the students' triumphal song.

Talking to Persuade

— Peng Nian

There are originally no relatives and friends in the world, and even if there are, it is only when you are successful and powerful. Because the affection of relatives and friends is built on money.

Flattery is the most valuable thing. If a person does not have the art of flattery, no matter how proficient your talent and learning are, you will still be following in someone else's footsteps, and there is no hope of becoming a big shot.

If a person cherishes public property as much as private property, then public property will not be damaged.

The sweet time for the working class is at night, but the sweet time for the aristocratic class is in the morning. Because the working class is producing all day long, while the aristocratic class is still dreaming sweet dreams.

If all the expenses for weddings and funerals in the country were donated to refugees, then the refugees could at least get a day of comfort.

If we recognize that there is a country, and everyone fulfills their obligations a little, then the three northeastern provinces would not have been taken away by the violent Japanese.

The advertising power of Shanghai is truly greater than that of small cities. Because Shanghai is vast and densely populated, there are many similar businesses, so customers only recognize the advertisements in the newspapers, which are the businesses where they need to buy things.

The women of Shanghai are truly comical. Upper body in a leather-collar coat, lower body in shorts above the knees, and a thin silk cheongsam underneath the coat. What comical, what contradiction!

If the child beggars beside the tram stop are given a good education, can they not find pearls and gems in the trash can?

If college students put the effort of studying love into books, then all college students could become masters and bachelors.

High-ranking officials despise low-ranking officials as if they were even smaller than mosquitoes. This is because their vision is too great. Because they only know that there are superiors.

Page 21

If the manager's stern face towards the shop assistants is seen by members of the League of Nations, they will surely say that China is a country that is exhausting its people and engaging in military aggression.

If resisting foreign aggression was as enthusiastic as internal warfare, then Japan would have already been annexed by China.

If a person was as good as the obituary says they were, then China would have simply no corrupt officials, local bullies, or thieves acting as such.

In a store, the manager's monthly salary is eighty yuan, while the shop assistant's monthly salary is only six yuan. From this, it seems that only the manager has parents and children, and the shop assistant has no family.

Life?

— Nankong

Dong suddenly came to my residence, which was an unexpected excitement and joy for me. At the same time, he was also very happy and talked a lot, from his situation after we separated to the dryness of life, from social issues to national affairs, to the mention of the September 18th Incident and the Shanghai Battle. Resentment and indignation surged in our minds, and we felt that life was bleak! Especially for us in this situation of internal worries and external troubles coming one after another, the pain inflicted by "national crisis" and "family sorrow"!

"Gong! Don't you know that Wen is dead?" Dong sadly told me, with infinite regret showing in his eyelashes. His mood was serene. At the same time, Wen's sallow and thin face, round eyes, hidden in the deep recess under his eyebrows, and high cheekbones, which never showed a trace of a smile, were deeply imprinted in my mind. Now he has tragically passed away and bid us farewell forever! No! He has gone to the happy paradise!

Wen's experiences were indeed too tragic. His father abandoned him and his mother five years after he was born and died. The remaining inheritance was not enough to pay for the cost of a meal for the bourgeoisie. Fortunately, his mother's hard work maintained their livelihood and cultivated him for several years of schooling. Later, thanks to the promotion of relatives and friends, he was finally apprenticed in a store. Because of the poverty of his family, he was able to work very diligently, but unfortunately his mother did not wait for him to provide for her and followed in his father's footsteps. Grief struck his heart, and he felt that the good luck he had encountered was too cruel and dark.

After struggling through hardship and difficult struggles, he finally managed to revive the family foundation. However, the evil disease, tuberculosis, was entangling him. Driven by life, he did not have the ability to rest and recuperate. His meager income was only enough for the clothing and food of his wife and children. He still ran around in the wind and frost. In his constant coughing, he could often find chunks of bloody sputum. On his frowning yellow face, he became increasingly pale and thin. He knew that this was an express lane to hasten the end of his life and step into the tomb, but the lash of life could not but make him run around, otherwise! He would become a starving corpse!

In the dimly lit, low-ceilinged room, the orphan, not yet three years old, was curled up in his mother's arms, crying. The young widow, with her brows tightly locked, shed tears like beads falling from a string, and sobbed sadly as she looked down at Wen's portrait!

Shop Assistant Communication

Specific Methods for Amateur Organizations

Mr. Editor:

After reading Mr. Hong Mingchang's small suggestion, he not only sighs passively, but also actively thinks of ways, which is very correct. If some young people have this spirit, not only can their own problems be solved, but the problems of the entire nation can also be solved. However, the two methods he put forward are actually only one, which is "contacting feelings and studying knowledge with each other." Simply having such empty methods is still not very useful. How exactly do we contact feelings? How exactly do we study knowledge with each other? Before we get concrete methods, I am afraid that the so-called contacting feelings is just getting to know each other, and the so-called studying knowledge is just meeting and talking. Therefore, we must have practical methods for everyone to study knowledge, in other words: there must be an organization. Here, I would like to put forward one of my opinions over the years and discuss it with everyone.

Last year, I planned to organize a Youth Hardship Study Association, wanting to imitate the method of correspondence courses, but without students paying fees. The declaration and articles of association had already been drafted, and I went to discuss it with several professors. Naturally, they usually also chanted the tune of seeking benefits for society, but when I mentioned that they should purely fulfill their obligations to undertake this kind of correspondence teaching, some were perfunctory, and some simply said that in Shanghai, it is not good to do things without money. Immediately afterwards, the "January 28th" incident suddenly occurred. My place of residence was in the war zone, and the drafts of the declaration and articles of association were also lost. Because of my livelihood, I was running around, and I invisibly put this matter aside.

Now that Mr. Hong wants to seriously study knowledge with each other, there must be such an organization. No matter what the name and method of the organization are, a correspondence school that does not charge tuition is most suitable for the environment of poor young people. Although some professors may not be willing to do such a purely voluntary thing, if you hire them in the name of your newspaper, they may not refuse. In case they refuse, then we must change the method, that is, if your newspaper is willing to take the responsibility of providing practical guidance, then this voluntary teaching must be borne by you. It is best to open a special column, such as: "Youth Lecture" or "Poor Youth School". Explain the questions they raise; and tell them how to study, or what to study; and sometimes you can gather them together at a certain time and place to have a sincere talk on the one hand, and examine their character and habits on the other hand, and then give further guidance. In the current Chinese society, schools have become the monopoly of a few people.

And most young people are disappointed, wandering, and even falling into depravity and suicide. The responsibility for this education must be borne by the news media, otherwise the danger of individual future will be the danger of the entire society's future, how important is the relationship!

Naturally, the opinions I have stated above may have some difficult points, but as long as this principle is adhered to, then the method of changing is not a problem.

I am a shop assistant, and I deeply feel the pain of being out of school, so I fully agree with Mr. Hong's suggestion, so I put forward a more practical method. But I also hope that you can give a satisfactory solution.

Zhu Ying December 14th

Novel

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (Continued - 8)

— Qin Shouou

In this world, no matter what the matter, once you discover a small flaw, many big loopholes will be found out for you without any effort. First, I merely felt the boredom and vexation of home life. Then, the mocking cold words of my stepmother, the mischief of my younger brothers... all kinds of dissatisfactions piled up before my eyes.

Barely enduring the Gregorian New Year, I still held a vibrant and active heart and returned to Shanghai. As soon as I stopped my journey, the first thing I did was call you. Alas! This one phone call negated all the hard work I had put in over forty or fifty days!

In light of these two failures, even though my body was so exhausted on the day of my departure—burning hot all over and as weak as a dead man’s limbs—I endured the pain with a spirit of great sacrifice, fought back the illness, and resolutely took the night train on the Beijing-Shanghai line, leaving Shanghai, leaving your Shanghai, and departing.

Apart from you, there was nothing in Shanghai worth my lingering over. However, it was Shanghai that bestowed innocence upon me; it was also Shanghai that allowed me to truly understand the meaning of life; it was Shanghai that, out of nowhere, pushed you into my longing thoughts, adding such a poignant and bittersweet episode to my life, a story that made me both laugh and cry. In the twenty-five years I’ve lived, the many farces I have performed, the most joyful, the most painful, and the most deeply stimulating, all took place in Shanghai. Therefore, at this final farewell, no matter how dark or sordid its original face may be, I cannot help but feel a bit downhearted.

The Beijing-Shanghai line night train departed at 11 o’clock as usual. At 10:48, I squeezed my weak, like a stove cat, body into the half of the train station that barely survived the mercy of the Great Japanese Air Force bombs.

The reason for my delayed arrival was not that my sacrificial courage had been hindered, but that my conscience suddenly had a deeper revelation. I felt that no matter how unworthy my family was of my attachment, my father, my wife, my daughter, they were, after all, in the position of creditors towards me—creditors of love! How could I quietly leave and completely shirk my debts?

I didn't plan to leave a single word to my family. If I had to leave anything, then only the four words "deserves ten thousand deaths" would be most fitting and sincere. Anything beyond that would inevitably be contrived. Rather than that, I wouldn't write anything! So, my conscience made a discovery, but I didn't leave a letter. Since I wasn't leaving a letter, I had to find something else that could represent the meaning of leaving a letter.

Naturally, this would only be material compensation.

Last year, didn’t I write a book called “Observations on International Trade,” published by the ×× Bookstore? On that manuscript, dear little friend, I remember you also wrote several lines! The price of this one great work of Zhu Jinchi’s entire life, although I had fought for it like it was human life and got it up to eight hundred yuan, but later, the introducer left, and this money never reached my pocket. I could have given up these small rights. For me, these sacrifices would not have caused any feeling at this point, but in order to repay my father, wife, and daughters in case of any need, I had to apologize to the big boss. I used extremely stern methods and, within four or five hours, recovered these eight hundred good silver dollars. Along with the many clothes and hats I had left behind, they all became my legacy when I left. Perhaps my family has already fully received them at this moment.

Whether such an arrangement can give my father, wife, and daughters some comfort, or whether it will increase their pain even more, is something I cannot control.

Film Special

Overseas News

Hollywood's Postmen (Part 2)

— Guang Yi

In the past, many letters were sent to Hollywood with only "It" written on the envelope, and the postman would deliver it to Clara Bow. Others, such as those addressed to "Mr. Benllur," would be sent to Ramon Novarro. Letters addressed to "The Man of a Thousand Faces" were given to Lon Chaney, who is now deceased.

William Boyd received a letter addressed to "The Cop," which was a role he had played in a film. In addition, letters addressed to "Tony" were sent to Tom Mix.

David Lee, a young star at Fox Studios, was too young to read his own mail, but he received many letters every day, which were opened and handled by his mother. Once, he received a small red letter containing nothing but a drawing of a rabbit.

Some fans wrote to "Leo," which was the name of the lion in the Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer logo. Others wrote to the cocky rooster in the Pathe company logo.

According to a statistic, approximately 885,000 fan letters are sent to Hollywood each month. Paramount alone receives an average of 197,000 letters each month. Some of these letters are sent by airmail.

Fans often include their addresses on the envelopes and write "Return to Sender if Undeliverable." However, the postmen are happy to do their best to identify the stars they are trying to reach from the strange and peculiar addresses on the letters. The stars who receive the letters rarely say that they were misdelivered.

Film Review

On "Jade Face Disaster"

— Ming

The name "Jade Face Disaster" (Convicted), which premiered at the Nanjing Grand Theatre yesterday, sounds so romantic and alluring, but the content is not so alluring. It would be better to use a direct translation or a more detective-oriented title that is more accurate.

The content is as follows: On a ship, a solitary actress is pursued by two men, one a musician, the other a great detective. The musician is killed, and the evidence clearly points to the woman as the murderer. However, the great detective uses every method to find the real culprit, who turns out to be a crew member on the ship, who committed the crime due to a monetary grudge. As a result, the detective and the actress become good companions.

This film cannot be called bad. Many short segments include both detective work and love, and it is certainly not easy to take care of every aspect.

The male lead, Jameson Thomas, is silent, eloquent, and moves in a way that befits the identity of a great detective, but his expressions are sometimes insufficient. The female lead, Aileen Pringle, does a good job. Although there are only a few close-ups, they are still very good. However, it is not appropriate that she is portrayed as an actress in the film. I think it would be better if she were just a woman traveling or an employee going to work, because she really doesn't have the "skill" of an actress. Richard Tucker, who plays the musician, is commendable. He performs the personality of the villain well and can be called "skilled." Many supporting actors are also watchable.

A film often shows some sea views, not forgetting that it is a story on a ship, and there are also ingenious branches inserted to adjust, which is certainly the director's care. However, he—the director—neglected the overall structure. With such a plot and competent actors, he made something that could have been tense into something ordinary. The film's core is based on "detective work," and there are many places where techniques could have been used to create a stimulating and mysterious masterpiece, but everything was destroyed by him, which is a great pity.

There are many supporting actors, and their roles are also complicated, so the main characters are often submerged, making the audience's spirits relax, and the film becomes very scattered.

The sound is good and not too lengthy, but at the first screening in Nanjing yesterday, there was a lot of noise in the first four reels, and the sound tape was even damaged by the projector. I believe this is not the fault of the film, and the Nanjing machine room should be more careful.

Overall, I think it is watchable, but it certainly won't give you the tense shivers like the advertisements say, and there is no "mysterious and winding" "fog of uncertainty" placed before you.

Am I to Be a Fish?

— Xing

There is a saying in Hollywood: "If the mermaid on the sandy beach is as beautiful as Gloria Stuart plays her, then men all over the world would join the navy and be willing to be a sailor." Indeed, her healthiness and sparkling blonde hair are enough to make anyone fall in love.

Recently, many people in Hollywood were disappointed because she has married a successful young sculptor. Of course, this makes anyone jealous and envious.

Little Fairbanks and Joan Crawford

— Xing

Little Fairbanks and Joan Crawford are a well-known couple, the most famous and perfect couple in Hollywood. Although many newspapers have campaigned against them, saying they are going to divorce, this rampant trend in Hollywood has not affected them. Little Fairbanks belongs to United Artists, and his recent film is "War Nurse", which was shown at the Carlton last month. Joan Crawford, however, is a basic star of MGM. Her recent films are "Letty Lynton", which was shown at the Cathay, and "Grand Hotel", which is about to be shipped overseas. The two have never co-starred. During the American general election this year, Joan was the second queen out of tens of thousands of people.

Tidbits from the Film Stage

"Capturing the Spirit, Neglecting the Appearance"—Joan Crawford's Imitation of Greta Garbo

— Olive

Greta Garbo's profound performance, intense emotions, and bewitching movements have left an indelible impression on anyone who has seen her films.

Many people in Hollywood imitate her style, but most of them "neglect the spirit and capture the appearance," with no charm. Joan Crawford, after years of effort, has been able to obtain Garbo's charm.

She can take Garbo's excellent qualities and apply them to what suits her, while abandoning everything that is not suitable. For example, Garbo's hair is praised by people, and Joan Crawford, because her face shape and eyes are similar to Garbo's, adopted Garbo's style. In the dialogue section, Joan Crawford knows that her raw American accent is more pleasant to listen to than Garbo's hoarse voice, so she still uses her own voice.

In fact, in the eyes of critics, Joan Crawford is indeed someone who can imitate Garbo and capture her spirit. Joan Crawford does not blindly imitate Garbo; she can develop her own personality that has not been fully developed. In each new film, anyone can notice her amazing progress. It is said that in the film "Grand Hotel," she has the same performance as Garbo.

New Film Introduction

"The Bitter Tea of General Yen" (Part 1)

— Crane

Hollywood-made films about Chinese society, such as Marlene Dietrich's "Shanghai Express" or Rock's "The Bitter Tea of General Yen", have many inaccuracies or excesses, so Chinese people always feel that people intentionally insult our nation and must be overthrown.

This kind of thinking has long been buried in our minds. When the news of "The Bitter Tea of General Yen" being filmed came to China, before we knew its content, we always felt some suspicion in our hearts: is there anything insulting to our country in it?

Now, the November issue of ScreenRomance has published its full text. After reading it in detail, I feel that there is nothing detrimental or insulting to our country.

The plot is as follows: An American girl named Megan Davis travels from Boston to Shanghai, preparing to marry her former classmate and lover, Dr. Robert Strike, a missionary in Shanghai. At the time, there was a war in Zhabei, and Dr. Strike was busy with relief work for the refugees, so the wedding was postponed. She agreed and joined the relief work herself.

One day, she and Bob set out to rescue orphans, but were unfortunately scattered by the chaotic soldiers, and she was knocked down and fainted. When she woke up, she was in General Yen's mansion, where she met General Yen's concubine, Mrh-Li. Because the road was unsafe, General Yen kept her there.

Mrh-Li was having an affair with an adjutant and was sentenced by General Yen to be shot the next morning. Megan mourned her life and resented General Yen's tyranny. She went to General Yen to plead for mercy on her behalf. General Yen told her that "This is not because of my jealousy or revenge, but because she is suspected of leaking military secrets to the enemy." After a considerable amount of conversation and pleading, General Yen finally agreed, but Megan must be a hostage.

The gentle General Yen touched Megan's heart. Since then, Megan no longer felt that General Yen was as tyrannical as the Chinese warlord she had imagined in her mind. A friendship had developed between them. (To be continued)

Film Industry Investigation

A Look at the Three Major Companies

— Ji Shen

When it comes to the domestic film industry, Lianhua, Tianyi, and Mingxing are the three most important companies. Today, I will not go into details, but just record them one by one for the reference of film fans. I hope that those who know will not consider me meddlesome.

(1) Capital: In the economically bankrupt Chinese film industry, Tianyi, Lianhua, and Mingxing can be considered leaders. At the beginning, Lianhua had a set capital of two million, but the actual receipt was less than half of that. Any shortfall was fully borne by Luo Mingyou personally. Currently, Lianhua has a total of five major studios in Hong Kong, Shanghai, and Peiping. The total assets are over one million. Mingxing, with its deep qualifications and years of surplus, has a perfect economic situation. Their organization is not like Lianhua, with Mr. Luo personally responsible. The amount of capital depends entirely on the enthusiasm of the shareholders. In urgent times, the board of directors will also find temporary solutions. As for Tianyi Company, it was originally the personal property of Mr. Shao Zuiweng. So, to know about Tianyi's capital, just look at Mr. Shao's private property. At present, Tianyi's capital has also exceeded 500,000 national currency.

(2) Business: In these trading ports of Beijing, Tianjin, Peiping, Shanghai, Hankou, and Hong Kong, there is no doubt that Lianhua has taken the first place, especially the so-called representative work "Humanity." The Ping'an Theater in Peiping, which never screened domestic films, actually made an exception to screen it. The Xinguang, which never screened silent films in this city, screened it for seven days and then added three more days. When it was the turn of Guanghua, it was screened for 17 consecutive days. However, Lianhua's films were not doing well in Southeast Asia. The once sensational "Love and Duty" could not find ten people upstairs and downstairs at the time of its premiere. (Luo Mingyou's report at Lianhua last year). Mingxing's films, because they cater to the tastes of the middle and lower classes, indeed have an advantage in business. A group of business grandmothers feel that they must watch Mingxing films. In the past, "The Burning of the Red Lotus Temple" was the most popular domestic film, but the "A Laughing Affair," which the authorities intended to make a lot of money from, turned out to be mediocre. As for the business of Tianyi's films, on the whole, the situation is still good, but it is somewhat behind the time when they first filmed sound films last year.

(3) Talent: Regarding talent, Lianhua has many newcomers, Mingxing has many old people, and Tianyi has many new drama characters on the stage. However, recently, Mingxing and Tianyi have also been working hard to make progress, vigorously cultivating talent. Lianhua has eleven directors, Mingxing has eight, and Tianyi is very deserted. Recently, Li Pingqian left him again, which made him even more desolate. The number of screenwriters and photographers is still average, with no significant difference.

(4) Production: The company with the most productions is Mingxing. Tianyi and Lianhua also have a large number of productions. If you count them annually, Lianhua is no less than Mingxing, but Lianhua has five major studios and cannot surpass Mingxing, which only has one studio. Regarding this point, the order is Mingxing, Tianyi, Lianhua.

(5) Results: To talk about a company's results, you must think from the overall perspective. So, regarding the results of the films, Lianhua has firmly occupied the top position. From "Spring Dream in the Old Capital" to the recent "Struggle," we can fully understand that Lianhua's films are indeed better. The biggest disadvantage of Mingxing's film results is that they do not advance but stick to the old, and always maintain the attitude of the old brand. However, they also have their advantages, that is, they will not produce very bad films. As for the results of Tianyi, although they are not as good as before, according to the recent trends, the three companies have the determination to work hard, everyone is seizing art, following the times, and moving towards the path of success.

There are countless other issues about the three companies, and I will report to the readers another day.

Gao Zhanfei is Going to Hong Kong

— Xing Su

Gao Zhanfei was originally a basic actor in the second factory of Lianhua Company. Now, he is also playing the leading role in the sound film "Spring Tide" produced by Hengsheng Company. He is really busy with his work. When United Artists hired actors in Shanghai, he was also on the list of those invited, and the contract has been signed. However, many of the directors and actors invited by United Artists have now arrived in Hong Kong, preparing to start work. Only he has not finished the films on both sides of Lianhua and Hengsheng and cannot leave. United Artists has urged him several times, and he really cannot delay any longer, so he decided to depart for Hong Kong on the 17th. He has sent letters to Lianhua and Hengsheng, limiting the completion of his films to before the 15th.

Film Monographs

The Qualifications a Good Actor Must Possess

— Chen Dabe

You must be able to freely control and manipulate every subtle expression of yours. This is the qualification that every good actor must possess. This is also the unique ability of a performing artist. Who among all human beings cannot laugh? Who cannot cry? Everyone can cry and laugh. Everyone can make appropriate expressions when necessary. Everyone can unintentionally make extremely beautiful and artistic expressions. Why can't they be called performing artists? Why can only you enjoy this reputation on the screen? This is because you can freely control and manipulate every subtle expression of yours, and people who have not been trained cannot.

The crying and laughing that we have just practiced are the most basic and simplest expressions, but it is not easy to practice to the point where you can freely control and manipulate them. You have to cry like you are really crying, and laugh like you are really laughing. You certainly cannot be unmoved. But once you are moved, you lose the ability to freely control. This is something that everyone can understand without testing. For example, when you are acting in a sound film, you start laughing and can no longer follow the director's predetermined plan to continue speaking or make another expression within a few seconds, or cry profusely. No matter what, you cannot continue working according to the predetermined plan, and the company will waste a lot of film for you. This is still a good analogy. If you can't cry when you should cry, or you don't laugh when you should laugh, this loss is even greater. If you often make people suffer this loss, are you still embarrassed to be called an artist?
